# Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus

Morokei enclosed in an energy shield, wielding the Staff of Magnus

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian").
2. Kill the dragon priest [Morokei](/wiki/Skyrim:Morokei_(creature) "Skyrim:Morokei (creature)").
3. Retrieve the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus").

### To Save the College

A ghostly image of Savos and his companions

After the [Containment](/wiki/Skyrim:Containment "Skyrim:Containment") quest, you must leave the [college](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") at [Mirabelle Ervine's](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") behest, outfitted with the [Torc of Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Torc_of_Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Torc of Labyrinthian") and [Savos Aren's Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren%27s_Amulet "Skyrim:Savos Aren's Amulet"). Your destination is [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian"), which will be marked on your map, where you must retrieve the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus") in order to contain the [Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Lore:Eye_of_Magnus "Lore:Eye of Magnus").

Labyrinthian sits nestled in a pass through the mountains southeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). It can be approached from the north or south end of the pass.
Following the quest marker, at the top of one of the many staircases, you will arrive at the *Ceremonial Door*, which is the entrance to the ruin's interior. Here a ghostly after-image of a younger [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") and five adventurous mages from the college, [Atmah](/wiki/Skyrim:Atmah "Skyrim:Atmah"), [Girduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Girduin "Skyrim:Girduin"), [Takes-In-Light](/wiki/Skyrim:Takes-In-Light "Skyrim:Takes-In-Light"), [Hafnar Ice-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafnar_Ice-Fist "Skyrim:Hafnar Ice-Fist") and [Elvali Veren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elvali_Veren "Skyrim:Elvali Veren"), will appear. Apparently, the late Arch-Mage had explored the ruins before and the apparitions will replay their experience as you progress through the ruins.

### Labyrinthian

The [Skeletal Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeletal_Dragon "Skyrim:Skeletal Dragon")

The Labyrinthian indoor ruins are fairly straightforward and guarded by a number of [undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead"). The entrance room is littered with skeleton corpses; at the opposite end of the room, on your right, you will find a [spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes") on an altar.

Proceed through a passage leading to a closed gate opening on a wide room. Levers on each side of the gate can be used to raise it, but it will fall down after a few seconds. A number of skeletons await beyond the gate, as well as a [Skeletal Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeletal_Dragon "Skyrim:Skeletal Dragon"). It is possible to raise the gate and shoot through the open entrance without entering. You can thus eliminate the skeletons and even the dragon before going into the room.

In addition, the dragon doesn't seem to be able to fit through the gate, so if you have entered, you can retreat back through it to take cover. Loot the cavern and descend the stairs where another ghostly scene will relay the events of Girduin's death. Take a moment to read the etched tablet introducing visitors to the great city of [Bromjunaar](/wiki/Lore:Bromjunaar "Lore:Bromjunaar"), then proceed into the Labyrinthian Chasm.

Opening the door, you will find twin staircases leading down. Check the alcove on the right for a hidden chest, then take the right-hand staircase down. When you emerge into the chamber you will hear Morokei's voice, resonating with glowing power, addressing you in the [dragon language](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_Language "Lore:Dragon Language") "Wo meyz wah dii vul junaar?".

As he speaks, a large portion of your magicka will drain. As his voice subsides, a closed door is apparent. The door seems to be covered in ice, and then, as if to confirm, a [frost spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Spirit "Skyrim:Frost Spirit") will emerge from the doorway. A [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") is also standing in one of the alcoves in this room. After removing the enemies, locate a [flames spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Flames "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Flames") which is in an alcove nearby. Cast a [flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames") spell at the icy door to melt the ice crystals and open the door.

Entering the chasm beyond, Morokei will again address you, draining your magicka: "Nivahriin muz fent siiv nid aaz het". From the doorway, you will see a draugr standing below; an easy target for a ranged attack. There are several more draugr roaming this area, so be on guard. After eliminating the threat, enter the tunnel to find a door guarded by a [lightning rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Rune "Skyrim:Lightning Rune"). Behind the door, another draugr is in a small room with the [Equilibrium spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Equilibrium "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Equilibrium").

Return to the chasm and descend another level. There are several more draugr roaming this area, so be on guard. Here, the passageway will fork, with a bridge in front of you and a side passage continuing deeper into the chasm. You will hear Morokei's voice once again, this time speaking in your "guttural" language, trying to engage you in conversation.

Either path, across the bridge or along the side wall, lead to the bottom of the chasm; however, the bridge features more draugr. Beyond, the cave leads to a river running through the chasm. A door at the far end of the passage leads to the next section of the ruins. Approaching the door, you hear Morokei plaintively asking for Aren.

### Labyrinthian Thoroughfare

Once inside open the next gate that leads to a sunken cavern strewn with stalactites and stalagmites. Haunting this cavern is a skeleton and a draugr. Once you eliminate them, you can either open a novice-locked gate to the west, or take a passage to the north. If you open the gate take a few steps downstream and turn right. Travel through the small room and proceed onward.

If you take the passage to the north, you will arrive at the same place after meeting a skeleton. As you travel through, Morokei speaks to you once again, this time taunting you as your magicka drains away.

The next large room you come to is occupied by a troll. There are three barred windows providing a view of the next multi-leveled cavern. The entrance to this cavern is located to the right of these windows. In the next cavern, you will hear from Morokei goading you once again.

You will battle more skeletons as you descend into the cavern. At the first landing is a bridge heading west. This leads to a small room with two trolls and a chest. Go down the second set of stairs to the lever-controlled gate.

When you approach the gate, Morokei will again speak to you, this time recognizing that you are not Savos Aren. As Morokei has depleted your magicka again, wait for it to regenerate, if you wish, before opening the gate. Beyond the gate you will find skeletons and a swarm of wisps as well as a [wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp").

If you turn left through the gate, keep turning left and you will find 2 well-hidden flights of stairs in a corner; at the top are two skeletons (including a magic-user), an unlocked chest and a random aversion potion. You can jump over a dividing wall to kill/loot the skeletons if necessary, or just leave them be. Climb back down the stairs to ground level when you're done and proceed.

Go up a short flight of stairs in the west corner and across the raised dais to a door sealed with fire. As you approach, you will hear Morokei acknowledge that your power feeds his own, and then a [fire spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Spirit "Skyrim:Fire Spirit") will spawn and attack.

Once the spirit is dead, cast a frost spell on the door to open it. If you do not yet have a frost spell, a [Frostbite spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Frostbite "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Frostbite") or ice-based scrolls can be found on a round table to the left of the door.

And then there were three...

Beyond this door you will find a short passage and a gate leading into a circular room. As you enter, another vision of young Savos Aren and his companions will appear, their numbers somewhat depleted by now.

The next room is guarded by a skeleton, a [Spectral Warhound](/wiki/Skyrim:Spectral_Warhound "Skyrim:Spectral Warhound") and a ghostly [draugr wight](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr_Wight "Skyrim:Draugr Wight"). Be careful as you approach; Morokei's voice invites you to your doom while draining your magicka once again. A cascade of water flows into a trap door in the floor, and there is a passage onwards.

Either the trap door or the passage lead to the same room below, however, if you open the trap door and do not land on the log to break your fall or otherwise protect yourself, the fall is likely to kill you. Through this tunnel system you will meet more draugr wights. Fighting through you will find the door leading to the next zone, Labyrinthian, Tribune.

### Labyrinthian, Tribune

Proceeding a short distance past the door, you will encounter two ghostly draugr wights, one of them a boss, and another spectral warhound. Around the next corner you will find a spell tome for [Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Steadfast Ward") on a podium.

Go down the stairs and into a room with three [spellcaster traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap") that will unleash powerful destruction spells at you. There is a frost rune on the floor midway down, and another guardian may await at the other end of the room.

Next, go up a short flight of stairs to a ledge overlooking another cavern with a small pool below and another draugr. To the left is a wooden ramp up to a room and two additional spectral draugr along with some loot. To the right is a dirt path leading down to the room below.

Exit the cave and at the end of the corridor you will find a skeleton shackled to a wall with a leveled dagger in its chest. To the left, an adept-locked gate leads to a few valuable items and the unique item [Ancient Helmet of the Unburned](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Helmet_of_the_Unburned "Skyrim:Ancient Helmet of the Unburned").

To the right is a set of iron doors. When you approach the doors, you will see the visual phenomenon of Morokei's voice, but no voice is heard. However, your magicka will be drained again.

Open the doors to see a throne facing away from you with a high-leveled draugr attended by a Spectral Warhound companion. Once the fight is over, you can approach the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") to the southwest of the throne to learn a word of the [Slow Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Slow_Time "Skyrim:Slow Time") shout.

On the opposite side of the room to the word wall, you can pass through the right side of the tree to find a chest hidden behind a rock.

After the throne room, you will enter a corridor with a series of columns on each side. Progress with care, as you will experience another magicka-draining effect, and activate a group of skeletons and ghostly draugr.

At the opposite end of the corridor, the ghostly Savos and a diminished band of his companions lament that not all of their number have made it this far. One of them mentions a feeling that the final trial lies beyond the next door, and they vow to stick together and move forward. Open the iron door to the south.

### The battle against the Dragon Priest

Two enthralled wizards holding Morokei with magic

As you enter the large room, Morokei is completely protected by an energy shield cast by two [enthralled wizards](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthralled_Wizard "Skyrim:Enthralled Wizard"). You will soon learn that they are two of Savos' companions that were sacrificed to keep the dragon priest contained so Savos could escape.

You need to remove the wizards and their casting in order to access Morokei. A variety of strategies and techniques can be used to win this encounter; suggestions and tips are below:

- The mages can be targeted from the corridor leading to the room, allowing you to replenish your resources before engaging Morokei. [Drainspell Bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Drainspell_Bow "Skyrim:Drainspell Bow") (from the ghostly draugr encountered in Labyrinthian) have been proven to be effective against the mages. You can also use the doorway to your advantage by opening and closing the doors when engaging Morokei.
- The platforms around the walls of the room provide elevated positions that should provide you with an edge in the fight. It is possible to climb the wall immediately to the left and approach from above. You can sneak attack both wizards and have a good vantage point to attack Morokei.
- Morokei can conjure a [storm atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Storm Atronach") and employs [Command Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Command_Daedra "Skyrim:Command Daedra") and seems to prefer ranged and magical attacks, avoiding fighting at close quarters. Most of his offensive spells are [shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Damage "Skyrim:Shock Damage") based, so equipping yourself with [enchanted items](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel#Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel") such as [Zahkriisos](/wiki/Skyrim:Zahkriisos_(item) "Skyrim:Zahkriisos (item)")'[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") and [Otar's masks](/wiki/Skyrim:Otar "Skyrim:Otar") or using [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Potions") to [resist shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Shock "Skyrim:Resist Shock") damage will severely hamper his attacks.
- It appears that if you can back him into the small pool in the room, he cannot get out of the water, which traps him, but he can still fight back.
- If you get his health down a bit, then switch to a low power constant-effect spell or staff (e.g. [Staff of Sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Sparks "Skyrim:Staff of Sparks")), he'll keep his costly ward spell up constantly and deplete his own magicka. When he runs out of magicka he's powerless.
- He can turn your summons against you. If he does, then you recast the summon and get a new one, he won't turn them more than once or twice. However, he cannot manipulate [Flaming Familiars](/wiki/Skyrim:Flaming_Familiar "Skyrim:Flaming Familiar"), acquired from [protecting](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Scroll_For_Anska "Skyrim:A Scroll For Anska") [Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:Anska "Skyrim:Anska") in [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins"), though completing that quest requires you to confront [another](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(creature) "Skyrim:Vokun (creature)") [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest").
- At a high enough level, it is possible to summon a [Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord") against Morokei; he cannot turn Dremora as he can Atronachs. Beware Morokei's range, and note that the first rank of the *Summoner* [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") perk is sufficient to close the distance between platforms.
- The Enthralled Wizards can be [frenzied](/wiki/Skyrim:Frenzy_(effect) "Skyrim:Frenzy (effect)") using [illusion spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion_Spells "Skyrim:Illusion Spells") and seem to be surprisingly resilient to Morokei's attacks. They can be used to soften him up or even kill him.
- [Spell Absorption](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Absorption "Skyrim:Spell Absorption") will cause Morokei's attacks to replenish your magicka rather than depleting it.
- You can also call on a mage-type follower, such as [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") or Erandur, to drain his magicka pool with lightning spells, or have them attack head-on while you flank the dragon priest.
- There are two platforms that the mages were standing on keeping Morokei imprisoned. If you stand on the higher platform, keeping a few feet from the edge so that you are between the pillars holding up the dragon head and use ranged attacks (preferably arrows poisoned with damage magicka regen) against him so that the lower half of his body is eclipsed by the small flame pits that hang over the edge, when he returns fire his lightning spells will scatter off of the surroundings leaving you completely unaffected with him under the impression that you are taking damage. If your follower is keeping him busy on the lower platform across from it so that he cannot come down the stairs this can make for a quick fight.
- He can be lured down the stairs to the exit, where he may become stuck at a point next to the stairs and be unable to path to you or return ranged attacks.

Once the dragon priest has been defeated, collect both [Morokei's mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Morokei_(item) "Skyrim:Morokei (item)") and the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus"). Your next objective will be to return to [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir").

### Problems at Home

Proceed through the door toward a shortcut out of Labyrinthian. Savos will again manifest, apologizing for sacrificing his companions to keep the Dragon Priest imprisoned, and swearing to seal the ruin. Unbar and open the wooden door.

As you open a gate to the next room, [Estormo](/wiki/Skyrim:Estormo "Skyrim:Estormo"), a [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") mage and associate of [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano"), will enter the room from the other side and block your path. He will tell you that he will take the Staff from you because Ancano wants it kept safe, and also wants you dead. Optionally defeat Estormo, and leave Labyrinthian.
Outside, you will not be able to fast travel to the College. The nearest destination to which you can fast travel is Winterhold. Once you arrive there, enter the gate to the College. You will find [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir"), along with [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda") and [Arniel Gane](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel_Gane "Skyrim:Arniel Gane") battling [magic anomalies](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Anomaly#Magic_Anomaly "Skyrim:Magic Anomaly").

Once the anomalies are gone, speak to Tolfdir. He tells you that Ancano's power is growing, and that they cannot stop him. He ruefully hopes your trip to Labyrinthian was worth it. If you ask about Mirabelle, Tolfdir will tell you that she is dead; killed while ensuring everyone's escape from Ancano. Tolfdir asks you to lead the group inside to deal with Ancano. This completes the quest and initiates [the Eye of Magnus quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus").

## Notes

- The magicka drain associated with Morokei's voice is scripted and always drains all your magicka, even if you used the Fortify Restoration exploit to create game-breaking Fortify Magicka items. It is completely unaffected by Resist Magic or Spell Absorption effects from potions or apparel.
- Some of the [optional quests](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction)#Optional_Quests "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") cannot be completed while this quest is active.
- Both of the [enthralled wizards](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthralled_Wizard "Skyrim:Enthralled Wizard") in Labyrinthian Tribune are male, despite the fact that there was a female wizard remaining at the end of Savos Aren's endeavor.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, addresses this issue. The appearances of the wizards now match Hafnar and Atmah.
- It is possible to bypass the part of the quest where you fight Estormo by backtracking through the dungeon instead of using the shorter exit path. The quest will progress normally after this is done.
- Estormo was at one point meant to have another Thalmor agent named [Muril](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_NPCs#Muril "Skyrim:Unused NPCs") with him.

## Bugs

- It is possible to receive two copies of the Staff of Magnus because a separate helper quest runs an EquipItem call on the base object instead of the alias reference.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Estormo's low agression will cause him to accept a yield. He may also flee combat and is no longer hostile after regaining enough health.
- Sometimes, the after-images of Savos and his companions will not engage in their intended dialogue, and stand still instead.
- One or more of the ghosts of Savos and his companions may be missing from their intended scenes.
- Morokei may not attack at all, simply floating towards you and not doing anything.
  -  Use the `prid 00086CF4` then `kill` [console commands](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to kill Morokei; the quest will advance directly to "Find the staff of Magnus".
- After killing the skeletal dragon, it will sometimes reanimate. **?**
- The quest may fail to start after completing [Containment](/wiki/Skyrim:Containment "Skyrim:Containment"), and even trying manually start or end it with the console will not work.
  - Try completing any quest related to Labyrinthian before starting Containment mission, for some unknown reasons the quest fails to start if there is another quest with marker pointing to Labyrinthian.
  -  Make sure that all of the NPCs in the College of Winterhold are still present and enabled; For example, you may not be able to find [Arniel](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel_Gane "Skyrim:Arniel Gane") because he is disabled. In order to solve this issue, simply open the console and type `prid <RefID>` then `enable` to re-enable a specific NPC.
- The loading screens for Labyrinthian were meant to stop once this quest is finished, but they never stop due to incorrect conditions governing this.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- This quest may fail to start if either [Arniel Gane](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel_Gane "Skyrim:Arniel Gane") or [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda") are unavailable (killed, disabled, etc). Their parts in this quest are optional so their aliases have been marked to indicate this. The same issue can also prevent [The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus") from starting as well.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.6, fixes this bug.
- If you leave Labyrinthian early on and then come back, Morokei will sometimes not talk to you at all as you advance through the dungeon, but the magicka drain effect will still happen. **?**

## Quest Stages

| The Staff of Magnus (MG07) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I need to retrieve the Staff of Magnus from within Labyrinthian and return with it to the College of Winterhold. Only the staff will help me put an end to Ancano's abuse of the Eye of Magnus. *Objective 10:* Enter Labyrinthian |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Find the Staff of Magnus |
| 50 |  | I have recovered the Staff of Magnus, and need to get it back to the College at once. *Objective 80:* Return to Tolfdir |
| 80 |  | *Objective 80:* Return to Tolfdir |
| 200 | ☑ | I have recovered the Staff of Magnus. |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 30:* Defeat the Dragon Priest  *Objective 40:* Retrieve the Staff of Magnus  *Objective 50:* Exit Labrynthian  *Objective 60:* Escape the Thalmor  *Objective 70:* Find a way out of Labrynthian |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 30, 40, 60, 70.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MG07 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MG07`.

# Skyrim:The Steed Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png) | Standing Stone: The Steed Stone ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Steed+Stone)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DoomstoneNorthernPineForest01 | |
| Region | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |
| Location | |
| Northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") East of [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") | |

The Steed Stone

**The Steed Stone** is one of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stone "Skyrim:Standing Stone") scattered across Skyrim.

It is located on top of a cliff to the northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), near [Ironback Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout").

## The Steed Stone

.jpg)

The Steed Stone, when activated

The Steed Stone in the Playroom (Skyrim VR)

Activating the Steed Stone will present this message: *"Those under the sign of The Steed can carry more and do not suffer a movement penalty from armor."*

Activating The Steed Stone will remove any Standing Stone effects previously obtained. It increases carry weight by 100 and removes movement penalty of armor. It also makes worn armor weigh nothing, making [heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") a viable option for many character types.

The stone is found at the top of a couple of flights of stairs on a stone structure. It is near the highest point on the mountain. To reach the standing stone the best place to start is beside the northeastern tower of [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") and head just off of due east slightly south, taking a gap between two rock formations and then heading directly towards the stone and climbing a couple of snow covered banks. It is possible to travel from the standing stone to [Ironback Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout"), but far harder to travel in the other direction due to the terrain. There are no ore veins or harvestable plants in the area around the standing stone.

## Notes

- When [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")'s [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") is active, this ability only gives an additional 50 carry weight.
- A Steed Stone also appears in the [playroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Playroom "Skyrim:Playroom") for [Skyrim VR](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_VR "Skyrim:Skyrim VR").

## Bugs

- The Stone's effect also reduces the weight of any piece of armor in the player's inventory that is the same base item as any piece being worn. For example, if the player has 10 Glass Armor in their inventory, equipping one will make all of them weightless. This remains true even if the worn armor is enhanced by smithing, enchanted and renamed.
- The Stone's effect can cause apparel, armor, and weapons that weigh more or less than what you have equipped to positively or negatively affect your encumbrance. Switching from a ranged or two-handed weapon to a staff or one-handed weapon and a shield can also affect your encumbrance and vice versa. **?**

# Skyrim:The Straw that Broke

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Discover what is plaguing [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi")'s mind.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi") |
| Location(s): | [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") |
| Reward: | Random rare [Ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi")) |
| ID: | FreeformIvarstead02 |

*"You live among the clouds now, dear Reyda!"*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Discover what is plaguing [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi")'s mind.
2. Find [Reyda's Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Reyda%27s_Necklace "Skyrim:Reyda's Necklace").
3. Return the necklace to Narfi.

### Grief

When you visit [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi") in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), you will quickly find that all is not well with him. Narfi lives in his parents' broken-down house across the river from the lumber mill. When speaking to him, you will notice that he has a mental disability and is very distraught over the disappearance of his sister, Reyda. He will mention that [Wilhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Wilhelm "Skyrim:Wilhelm"), the innkeeper at [Vilemyr Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilemyr_Inn "Skyrim:Vilemyr Inn"), told him Reyda would come back, and that he needs to say goodbye to his sister like he did his mother and father.

### Pity

When speaking to Wilhelm, he will tell you that Narfi is harmless, but in a state since his sister disappeared. Wilhelm, meaning well, told Narfi his sister would return one day, but actually fears Reyda was killed while searching for [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") from the river. He will point you in the direction of the small island to the east of Ivarstead, where you can then go look for Narfi's sister. There is a small barrow dungeon on that island, [Geirmund's Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirmund%27s_Hall "Skyrim:Geirmund's Hall"), and it seems like the obvious place to start.

### Truth

Though Wilhelm's supposition about Reyda's fate turns out to be correct his directions are inaccurate. Reyda's remains are not at the island, but can be found underwater just east of the southern bridge into town. Due to the current they may be difficult to access. Next to her remains are [her necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Reyda%27s_Necklace "Skyrim:Reyda's Necklace") and a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"); the satchel contains some gold and several random alchemical ingredients. Return the necklace to Narfi. You can tell him the truth about what happened to Reyda, or assure him she will come back. In either case, you will receive three random, rare ingredients, and Narfi will, for the most part, remain the same.

## Notes

- Narfi is the victim of the Dark Brotherhood quest [Kill Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Narfi "Skyrim:Kill Narfi"). Once you accept the assassin quest, it will be impossible to complete the Reyda quest successfully.
  - To complete both the Dark Brotherhood quest and the miscellaneous quest after accepting the contract from Nazir, you can use the console command "setstage DBsidecontract01 20" to be able to speak to Narfi about his sister. This will mark that you have killed Narfi while he is still alive, but you can simply kill him after completing his side quest to set you back on track, or use the console command "setstage DBsidecontract01 10" to set you back to the step where you have access to the relevant dialogue and must kill Narfi to continue.

## Bugs

- If you show Reyda's necklace to Wilhelm, his reaction is exactly the same as Narfi's: *"Reyda! You saw Reyda? Did you tell her Narfi cries? Did you tell her Narfi never said goodbye like mother and father?"*
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
  - Special Edition seems to have patched this. The dialogue option is no longer present. This might only apply to Xbox.
- If you take the necklace from Reyda's satchel before asking Wilhelm about Narfi, the quest will not update beyond the stage requiring you to find her remains even if you search the satchel again.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  -  The command `setstage FreeformIvarstead02 40` will do the work.
  - Dropping and retaking the necklace using the console command `player.drop 663da 1` while standing over the underwater satchel causes a quest update, fixing the quest.
- Narfi may quit dialogue without giving you a chance to tell him about Reyda's fate and finish the quest.
- Going straight to Reyda's corpse after accepting the quest instead of talking to Wilhelm will leave the log entry about asking Wilhelm in your miscellaneous quests tab even after the quest, and Wilhelm will have no topic about Reyda should you visit later. The only way to fix this is by returning the quest to an earlier stage by using the command `setstage FreeformIvarstead02 20` and redoing the quest in proper sequence.
-  Reyda's name is frequently misspelled as Rayda in the German translations of Narfi's dialogue. **?**
- Completing this quest would make Narfi unavailable to become a [farmhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmhand "Skyrim:Farmhand")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming "Skyrim:Farming").
  - Recruiting him to be a farmhand first is a workaround.

## Quest Stages

| The Straw that Broke (FreeformIvarstead02) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Ask Wilhelm about Reyda |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Locate Reyda's remains |
| 40 |  | *Objective 30:* Bring Reyda's Necklace to Narfi |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformIvarstead02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformIvarstead02`.

# Skyrim:The Stumbling Sabrecat

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Inn: The Stumbling Sabrecat ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Stumbling+Sabrecat)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| FortDunstad04 | |
| Region | |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | |
| Location | |
| [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

The Stumbling Sabrecat

**The Stumbling Sabrecat** is a [tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") within [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad").

The building is in the fort's parade ground. The owner, [Baral Sendu](/wiki/Skyrim:Baral_Sendu "Skyrim:Baral Sendu"), was apparently killed by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") occupying the fort.

## The Stumbling Sabrecat

The counter immediately on your left upon entering holds an empty [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and four loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on top. Underneath the counter is five [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), eight [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), three loose septims, and a bottle of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"). Against the west wall behind the counter is a set of shelves holding nine bottles of alto wine and six bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). There are a flight of stairs leading down to the cellar against the rear wall to the north.

The main part of the first room is used as the sitting area for the tavern with a few tables and chairs with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of alto wine, and a bunch of jazbay grapes on one and two bottles of Nord mead on one of the tables. An unowned, single bed sits in the southwestern corner. A fireplace in the middle of the east wall has a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front with three sets of [imperial light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Light Boots"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), and a bottle of wine sitting on the hearth. Above the fireplace is a weapon plaque holding a [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword") and above that is the mounted head of a sabre cat with a bottle of alto wine in its mouth (see [notes](#Notes)) and a [copper and onyx circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Copper_and_Onyx_Circlet "Skyrim:Copper and Onyx Circlet") on its head.

Downstairs are two bandits. There is a pile of firewood and a stack of barrels under the stairs. Farther to the right are two sets of shelves. The first is full of small barrels of mead while the second holds a [leather helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Helmet "Skyrim:Leather Helmet"), a set of [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), and a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"). A double bed with the body of the former owner of the tavern, Baral Sendu (with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") still in his neck), is still usable. There is a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") at the foot of the bed and an apprentice-locked chest to the right, against the south wall. Another [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel is in the southwestern corner with a cupboard to the right of that holding more clothes. To the right of the cupboard is a long wooden table with a random [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") potion, an iron dagger and four more loose septims, with a large vat to the right of the table.

## Notes

- The Stumbling Sabrecat is the only inn or tavern in the game that does not have a unique sign at its entrance.
- There is a mounted sabre cat's head above the fireplace with a bottle of alto wine in its mouth, presumably a reference to the tavern's name.
- After starting the Imperial questline, Sendu's body and the two bandits present in the basement are removed and the place is cleaned up. The same is true if the fort is cleared from bandits and occupied by Stormcloaks. Once this happens, the tavern can be used as a convenient player house; it has beds, cooking, and the dresser and cupboard in the basement are safe containers.

## Bugs

- The steel greatsword above the fireplace cannot be removed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  The Stumbling Sabrecat

# Skyrim:The Sweep Job

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Nephele](/wiki/User:Nephele "User:Nephele"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Dwarfmp](/wiki/User:Dwarfmp "User:Dwarfmp"), checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Steal three specific valuable items from a wealthy house.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward) |
| ID: | TGRHC |

The Golden Urn and the Jeweled Candlestick in Evette San's House

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") about sweep jobs.
2. Enter the targeted house and steal the items she names.
3. Return them to Vex for a reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After joining the Thieves Guild, [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") will tell you that she handles all the [burglary](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job"), [shill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shill_Job "Skyrim:The Shill Job"), sweep, and [heist](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heist_Job "Skyrim:The Heist Job") jobs. Ask her for a sweep job and she will inform you that one of Skyrim's citizens has three items that the guild covets.

Steal the three items that she specifies from the provided location, and return them to Vex for a leveled gold reward. One of the three items appears in the same location as where the item for [The Burglary Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job") is placed, the only effective difference between this quest and The Burglary Job is that this quest requires two additional items to be stolen from the house. The items are found in three different locations in the house, sitting out on shelves or tables. Your quest objective will update each time you obtain one of the required items. The possible items are:

- [Golden Ship Model](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Ship_Model "Skyrim:Golden Ship Model")
- [Golden Urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Urn "Skyrim:Golden Urn")
- [Jeweled Candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Candlestick "Skyrim:Jeweled Candlestick")
- [Jeweled Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Flagon "Skyrim:Jeweled Flagon")
- [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet")
- [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher")
- [Ornate Drinking Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ornate_Drinking_Horn "Skyrim:Ornate Drinking Horn")

The quest can send you to any wealthy house in the game, which amounts to 29 possible houses. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Nepos's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos%27s_House "Skyrim:Nepos's House") [Ogmund's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund%27s_House "Skyrim:Ogmund's House") [Smelter Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House") [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") | [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") [Marise Aravel's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel%27s_House House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Giordano's House") |

You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest; you also cannot kill anyone living in the house.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- If one of the house's occupants dies for any reason while the quest is active (even if you are not responsible), you will fail the quest.
- If you get arrested in a hold that is not where the house is located, the quest still fails.

## Bugs

- If you have already participated in the quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") it becomes impossible to enter some homes in Whiterun (the entrance to Heimskr's House is always blocked, while others should clean up after some time has passed). However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish).
  -  You can use the console command `coc`, followed by the editor id of the house.
- If you cancel a sweep quest, the items don't disappear from the house which can cause some overlap problems if the quest is assigned to that house again. If a jeweled goblet is a target and a golden urn was previously placed, the goblet will be unable to be picked up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `MarkForDelete`, then target the golden urn, this should reveal the jeweled goblet.

## Quest Stages

| The Sweep Job (TGRHC) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've been told to clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. I need to complete this job without killing any of the location's residents or getting caught and spending time in jail. *Objective 10:* Clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables (<Global=TGRHCValuablesStolen>/3) |
| 50 |  | I've cleared <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. *Objective 20:* Return the valuables to Vex |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully completed the job and received my share of the pay. |
| 250 | ☒ | By killing a resident at the task's location, I've failed this job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | During the course of this task, I was arrested and sent to the local jail. I've therefore failed the job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | Before the task could be completed, I decided to quit. I've therefore failed the job and forfeited any pay I might have received. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRHC stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGRHC`.

# Skyrim:The Sweep Job

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Nephele](/wiki/User:Nephele "User:Nephele"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Dwarfmp](/wiki/User:Dwarfmp "User:Dwarfmp"), checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Steal three specific valuable items from a wealthy house.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward) |
| ID: | TGRHC |

The Golden Urn and the Jeweled Candlestick in Evette San's House

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") about sweep jobs.
2. Enter the targeted house and steal the items she names.
3. Return them to Vex for a reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After joining the Thieves Guild, [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") will tell you that she handles all the [burglary](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job"), [shill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shill_Job "Skyrim:The Shill Job"), sweep, and [heist](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heist_Job "Skyrim:The Heist Job") jobs. Ask her for a sweep job and she will inform you that one of Skyrim's citizens has three items that the guild covets.

Steal the three items that she specifies from the provided location, and return them to Vex for a leveled gold reward. One of the three items appears in the same location as where the item for [The Burglary Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job") is placed, the only effective difference between this quest and The Burglary Job is that this quest requires two additional items to be stolen from the house. The items are found in three different locations in the house, sitting out on shelves or tables. Your quest objective will update each time you obtain one of the required items. The possible items are:

- [Golden Ship Model](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Ship_Model "Skyrim:Golden Ship Model")
- [Golden Urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Urn "Skyrim:Golden Urn")
- [Jeweled Candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Candlestick "Skyrim:Jeweled Candlestick")
- [Jeweled Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Flagon "Skyrim:Jeweled Flagon")
- [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet")
- [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher")
- [Ornate Drinking Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ornate_Drinking_Horn "Skyrim:Ornate Drinking Horn")

The quest can send you to any wealthy house in the game, which amounts to 29 possible houses. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Nepos's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos%27s_House "Skyrim:Nepos's House") [Ogmund's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund%27s_House "Skyrim:Ogmund's House") [Smelter Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House") [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") | [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") [Marise Aravel's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel%27s_House "Skyrim:Marise Aravel's House") [Romlyn Dreth's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth%27s_House "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth's House") [Snow-Shod Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Manor "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor") [Valindor's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor%27s_House "Skyrim:Valindor's House") | [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") [Jala's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Jala's House") [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House") | [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") |

You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest; you also cannot kill anyone living in the house.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- If one of the house's occupants dies for any reason while the quest is active (even if you are not responsible), you will fail the quest.
- If you get arrested in a hold that is not where the house is located, the quest still fails.

## Bugs

- If you have already participated in the quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") it becomes impossible to enter some homes in Whiterun (the entrance to Heimskr's House is always blocked, while others should clean up after some time has passed). However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish).
  -  You can use the console command `coc`, followed by the editor id of the house.
- If you cancel a sweep quest, the items don't disappear from the house which can cause some overlap problems if the quest is assigned to that house again. If a jeweled goblet is a target and a golden urn was previously placed, the goblet will be unable to be picked up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `MarkForDelete`, then target the golden urn, this should reveal the jeweled goblet.

| 50 |  | I've cleared <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. *Objective 20:* Return the valuables to Vex |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRHC stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. # Skyrim:The Sweep Job

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Nephele](/wiki/User:Nephele "User:Nephele"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Dwarfmp](/wiki/User:Dwarfmp "User:Dwarfmp"), checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Steal three specific valuable items from a wealthy house.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward) |
| ID: | TGRHC |

The Golden Urn and the Jeweled Candlestick in Evette San's House

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") about sweep jobs.
2. Enter the targeted house and steal the items she names.
3. Return them to Vex for a reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After joining the Thieves Guild, [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") will tell you that she handles all the [burglary](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job"), [shill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shill_Job "Skyrim:The Shill Job"), sweep, and [heist](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heist_Job "Skyrim:The Heist Job") jobs. Ask her for a sweep job and she will inform you that one of Skyrim's citizens has three items that the guild covets.

Steal the three items that she specifies from the provided location, and return them to Vex for a leveled gold reward. One of the three items appears in the same location as where the item for [The Burglary Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job") is placed, the only effective difference between this quest and The Burglary Job is that this quest requires two additional items to be stolen from the house. The items are found in three different locations in the house, sitting out on shelves or tables. Your quest objective will update each time you obtain one of the required items. The possible items are:

- [Golden Ship Model](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Ship_Model "Skyrim:Golden Ship Model")
- [Golden Urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Urn "Skyrim:Golden Urn")
- [Jeweled Candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Candlestick "Skyrim:Jeweled Candlestick")
- [Jeweled Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Flagon "Skyrim:Jeweled Flagon")
- [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet")
- [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher")
- [Ornate Drinking Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ornate_Drinking_Horn "Skyrim:Ornate Drinking Horn")

The quest can send you to any wealthy house in the game, which amounts to 29 possible houses. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Nepos's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos%27s_House "Skyrim:Nepos's House") [Ogmund's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund%27s_House "Skyrim:Ogmund's House") [Smelter Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House") [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") | [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") [Marise Aravel's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel%27s_House "Skyrim:Marise Aravel's House") [Romlyn Dreth's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth%27s_House "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth's House") [Snow-Shod Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Manor "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor") [Valindor's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor%27s_House "Skyrim:Valindor's House") | [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") [Jala's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Jala's House") [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House") | [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") |

You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest; you also cannot kill anyone living in the house.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- If one of the house's occupants dies for any reason while the quest is active (even if you are not responsible), you will fail the quest.
- If you get arrested in a hold that is not where the house is located, the quest still fails.

## Bugs

- If you have already participated in the quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") it becomes impossible to enter some homes in Whiterun (the entrance to Heimskr's House is always blocked, while others should clean up after some time has passed). However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish).
  -  You can use the console command `coc`, followed by the editor id of the house.
- If you cancel a sweep quest, the items don't disappear from the house which can cause some overlap problems if the quest is assigned to that house again. If a jeweled goblet is a target and a golden urn was previously placed, the goblet will be unable to be picked up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `MarkForDelete`, then target the golden urn, this should reveal the jeweled goblet.

## Quest Stages

| The Sweep Job (TGRHC) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've been told to clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. I need to complete this job without killing any of the location's residents or getting caught and spending time in jail. *Objective 10:* Clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables (<Global=TGRHCValuablesStolen>/3) |
| 50 |  | I've cleared <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. *Objective 20:* Return the valuables to Vex |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully completed the job and received my share of the pay. |
| 250 | ☒ | By killing a resident at the task's location, I've failed this job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | During the course of this task, I was arrested and sent to the local jail. I've therefore failed the job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | Before the task could be completed, I decided to quit. I've therefore failed the job and forfeited any pay I might have received. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRHC stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGRHC`.

Ask her for a sweep job and she will inform you that one of Skyrim's citizens has three items that the guild covets.

Steal the three items that she specifies from the provided location, and return them to Vex for a leveled gold reward. One of the three items appears in the same location as where the item for [The Burglary Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job") is placed, the only effective difference between this quest and The Burglary Job is that this quest requires two additional items to be stolen from the house. The items are found in three different locations in the house, sitting out on shelves or tables. Your quest objective will update each time you obtain one of the required items. The possible items are:

- [Golden Ship Model](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Ship_Model "Skyrim:Golden Ship Model")
- [Golden Urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Urn "Skyrim:Golden Urn")
- [Jeweled Candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Candlestick "Skyrim:Jeweled Candlestick")
- [Jeweled Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Flagon "Skyrim:Jeweled Flagon")
- [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet")
- [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher")
- [Ornate Drinking Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ornate_Drinking_Horn "Skyrim:Ornate Drinking Horn")

The quest can send you to any wealthy house in the game, which amounts to 29 possible houses. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Nepos's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos%27s_House "Skyrim:Nepos's House") [Ogmund's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund%27s_House "Skyrim:Ogmund's House") [Smelter Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House") [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") | [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") [Marise Aravel's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel%27s_House "Skyrim:Marise Aravel's House") [Romlyn Dreth's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth%27s_House "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth's House") [Snow-Shod Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Manor "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor") [Valindor's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor%27s_House "Skyrim:Valindor's House") | [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") [Jala's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Jala's House") [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House") | [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") |

You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest; you also cannot kill anyone living in the house.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- If one of the house's occupants dies for any reason while the quest is active (even if you are not responsible), you will fail the quest.
- If you get arrested in a hold that is not where the house is located, the quest still fails.

## Bugs

- If you have already participated in the quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") it becomes impossible to enter some homes in Whiterun (the entrance to Heimskr's House is always blocked, while others should clean up after some time has passed). However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish).
  -  You can use the console command `coc`, followed by the editor id of the house.
- If you cancel a sweep quest, the items don't disappear from the house which can cause some overlap problems if the quest is assigned to that house again. If a jeweled goblet is a target and a golden urn was previously placed, the goblet will be unable to be picked up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `MarkForDelete`, then target the golden urn, this should reveal the jeweled goblet.

## Quest Stages

| The Sweep Job (TGRHC) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've been told to clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. I need to complete this job without killing any of the location's residents or getting caught and spending time in jail. *Objective 10:* Clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables (<Global=TGRHCValuablesStolen>/3) |
| 50 |  | I've cleared <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. *Objective 20:* Return the valuables to Vex |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully completed the job and received my share of the pay. |
| 250 | ☒ | By killing a resident at the task's location, I've failed this job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | During the course of this task, I was arrested and sent to the local jail. I've therefore failed the job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | Before the task could be completed, I decided to quit. I've therefore failed the job and forfeited any pay I might have received. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRHC stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGRHC`.

# Skyrim:The Sweep Job

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Nephele](/wiki/User:Nephele "User:Nephele"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Dwarfmp](/wiki/User:Dwarfmp "User:Dwarfmp"), checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |
