# Skyrim:The Sweep Job

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Nephele](/wiki/User:Nephele "User:Nephele"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Dwarfmp](/wiki/User:Dwarfmp "User:Dwarfmp"), checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Steal three specific valuable items from a wealthy house.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward) |
| ID: | TGRHC |

The Golden Urn and the Jeweled Candlestick in Evette San's House

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") about sweep jobs.
2. Enter the targeted house and steal the items she names.
3. Return them to Vex for a reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After joining the Thieves Guild, [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") will tell you that she handles all the [burglary](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job"), [shill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shill_Job "Skyrim:The Shill Job"), sweep, and [heist](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heist_Job "Skyrim:The Heist Job") jobs. Ask her for a sweep job and she will inform you that one of Skyrim's citizens has three items that the guild covets.

Steal the three items that she specifies from the provided location, and return them to Vex for a leveled gold reward. One of the three items appears in the same location as where the item for [The Burglary Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job") is placed, the only effective difference between this quest and The Burglary Job is that this quest requires two additional items to be stolen from the house. The items are found in three different locations in the house, sitting out on shelves or tables. Your quest objective will update each time you obtain one of the required items. The possible items are:

- [Golden Ship Model](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Ship_Model "Skyrim:Golden Ship Model")
- [Golden Urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Urn "Skyrim:Golden Urn")
- [Jeweled Candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Candlestick "Skyrim:Jeweled Candlestick")
- [Jeweled Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Flagon "Skyrim:Jeweled Flagon")
- [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet")
- [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher")
- [Ornate Drinking Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ornate_Drinking_Horn "Skyrim:Ornate Drinking Horn")

The quest can send you to any wealthy house in the game, which amounts to 29 possible houses. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Nepos's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos%27s_House "Skyrim:Nepos's House") [Ogmund's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund%27s_House "Skyrim:Ogmund's House") [Smelter Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House") [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") | [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") [Marise Aravel's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel%27s_House "Skyrim:Marise Aravel's House") [Romlyn Dreth's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth%27s_House "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth's House") [Snow-Shod Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Manor "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor") [Valindor's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor%27s_House "Skyrim:Valindor's House") | [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") [Jala's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Jala's House") [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House") | [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") |

You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest; you also cannot kill anyone living in the house.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- If one of the house's occupants dies for any reason while the quest is active (even if you are not responsible), you will fail the quest.
- If you get arrested in a hold that is not where the house is located, the quest still fails.

## Bugs

- If you have already participated in the quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") it becomes impossible to enter some homes in Whiterun (the entrance to Heimskr's House is always blocked, while others should clean up after some time has passed). However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish).
  -  You can use the console command `coc`, followed by the editor id of the house.
- If you cancel a sweep quest, the items don't disappear from the house which can cause some overlap problems if the quest is assigned to that house again. If a jeweled goblet is a target and a golden urn was previously placed, the goblet will be unable to be picked up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `MarkForDelete`, then target the golden urn, this should reveal the jeweled goblet.

## Quest Stages

I need to complete this job without killing any of the location's residents or getting caught and spending time in jail. *Objective 10:* Clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables (<Global=TGRHCValuablesStolen>/3) |
| 50 |  | I've cleared <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. *Objective 20:* Return the valuables to Vex |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully completed the job and received my share of the pay. |
| 250 | ☒ | By killing a resident at the task's location, I've failed this job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | During the course of this task, I was arrested and sent to the local jail. I've therefore failed the job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRHC stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. # Skyrim:The Sweep Job

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Steal three specific valuable items from a wealthy house.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward) |
| ID: | TGRHC |

The Golden Urn and the Jeweled Candlestick in Evette San's House

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") about sweep jobs.
2. Enter the targeted house and steal the items she names.
3. Return them to Vex for a reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After joining the Thieves Guild, [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") will tell you that she handles all the [burglary](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job"), [shill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shill_Job "Skyrim:The Shill Job"), sweep, and [heist](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heist_Job "Skyrim:The Heist Job") jobs. Ask her for a sweep job and she will inform you that one of Skyrim's citizens has three items that the guild covets.

Steal the three items that she specifies from the provided location, and return them to Vex for a leveled gold reward. One of the three items appears in the same location as where the item for [The Burglary Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job") is placed, the only effective difference between this quest and The Burglary Job is that this quest requires two additional items to be stolen from the house. The items are found in three different locations in the house, sitting out on shelves or tables. Your quest objective will update each time you obtain one of the required items. The possible items are:

- [Golden Ship Model](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Ship_Model "Skyrim:Golden Ship Model")
- [Golden Urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Urn "Skyrim:Golden Urn")
- [Jeweled Candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Candlestick "Skyrim:Jeweled Candlestick")
- [Jeweled Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Flagon "Skyrim:Jeweled Flagon")
- [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet")
- [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher")
- [Ornate Drinking Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ornate_Drinking_Horn "Skyrim:Ornate Drinking Horn")

The quest can send you to any wealthy house in the game, which amounts to 29 possible houses. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Nepos's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos%27s_House "Skyrim:Nepos's House") [Ogmund's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund%27s_House "Skyrim:Ogmund's House") [Smelter Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House") [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") | [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") [Marise Aravel's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel%27s_House "Skyrim:Marise Aravel's House") [Romlyn Dreth's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth%27s_House "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth's House") [Snow-Shod Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Manor "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor") [Valindor's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor%27s_House "Skyrim:Valindor's House") | [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") [Jala's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Jala's House") [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House") | [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") |

You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest; you also cannot kill anyone living in the house.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- If one of the house's occupants dies for any reason while the quest is active (even if you are not responsible), you will fail the quest.
- If you get arrested in a hold that is not where the house is located, the quest still fails.

## Bugs

- If you have already participated in the quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") it becomes impossible to enter some homes in Whiterun (the entrance to Heimskr's House is always blocked, while others should clean up after some time has passed). However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish).
  -  You can use the console command `coc`, followed by the editor id of the house.
- If you cancel a sweep quest, the items don't disappear from the house which can cause some overlap problems if the quest is assigned to that house again. If a jeweled goblet is a target and a golden urn was previously placed, the goblet will be unable to be picked up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `MarkForDelete`, then target the golden urn, this should reveal the jeweled goblet.

## Quest Stages

| The Sweep Job (TGRHC) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've been told to clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. I need to complete this job without killing any of the location's residents or getting caught and spending time in jail. *Objective 10:* Clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables (<Global=TGRHCValuablesStolen>/3) |
| 50 |  | I've cleared <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. *Objective 20:* Return the valuables to Vex |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully completed the job and received my share of the pay. |
| 250 | ☒ | By killing a resident at the task's location, I've failed this job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | During the course of this task, I was arrested and sent to the local jail. I've therefore failed the job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | Before the task could be completed, I decided to quit. I've therefore failed the job and forfeited any pay I might have received. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRHC stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGRHC`.

- [Jeweled Candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Candlestick "Skyrim:Jeweled Candlestick")
- [Jeweled Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Flagon "Skyrim:Jeweled Flagon")
- [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet")
- [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher")
- [Ornate Drinking Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ornate_Drinking_Horn "Skyrim:Ornate Drinking Horn")

The quest can send you to any wealthy house in the game, which amounts to 29 possible houses. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Nepos's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos%27s_House "Skyrim:Nepos's House") [Ogmund's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund%27s_House "Skyrim:Ogmund's House") [Smelter Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House") [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") | [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") [Marise Aravel's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel%27s_House "Skyrim:Marise Aravel's House") [Romlyn Dreth's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth%27s_House "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth's House") [Snow-Shod Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Manor "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor") [Valindor's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor%27s_House "Skyrim:Valindor's House") | [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") [Jala's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Jala's House") [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House") | [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") |

You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest; you also cannot kill anyone living in the house.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- If one of the house's occupants dies for any reason while the quest is active (even if you are not responsible), you will fail the quest.
- If you get arrested in a hold that is not where the house is located, the quest still fails.

## Bugs

- If you have already participated in the quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") it becomes impossible to enter some homes in Whiterun (the entrance to Heimskr's House is always blocked, while others should clean up after some time has passed). However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish).
  -  You can use the console command `coc`, followed by the editor id of the house.
- If you cancel a sweep quest, the items don't disappear from the house which can cause some overlap problems if the quest is assigned to that house again. If a jeweled goblet is a target and a golden urn was previously placed, the goblet will be unable to be picked up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `MarkForDelete`, then target the golden urn, this should reveal the jeweled goblet.

## Quest Stages

| The Sweep Job (TGRHC) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've been told to clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. I need to complete this job without killing any of the location's residents or getting caught and spending time in jail. *Objective 10:* Clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables (<Global=TGRHCValuablesStolen>/3) |
| 50 |  | I've cleared <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. *Objective 20:* Return the valuables to Vex |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully completed the job and received my share of the pay. |
| 250 | ☒ | By killing a resident at the task's location, I've failed this job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | During the course of this task, I was arrested and sent to the local jail. I've therefore failed the job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | Before the task could be completed, I decided to quit. I've therefore failed the job and forfeited any pay I might have received. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRHC stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGRHC`.

# Skyrim:The Sweep Job

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Nephele](/wiki/User:Nephele "User:Nephele"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Dwarfmp](/wiki/User:Dwarfmp "User:Dwarfmp"), checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Steal three specific valuable items from a wealthy house.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward) |
| ID: | TGRHC |

The Golden Urn and the Jeweled Candlestick in Evette San's House

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") about sweep jobs.
2. Enter the targeted house and steal the items she names.
3. Return them to Vex for a reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After joining the Thieves Guild, [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") will tell you that she handles all the [burglary](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job"), [shill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shill_Job "Skyrim:The Shill Job"), sweep, and [heist](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heist_Job "Skyrim:The Heist Job") jobs. Ask her for a sweep job and she will inform you that one of Skyrim's citizens has three items that the guild covets.

Steal the three items that she specifies from the provided location, and return them to Vex for a leveled gold reward. One of the three items appears in the same location as where the item for [The Burglary Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job") is placed, the only effective difference between this quest and The Burglary Job is that this quest requires two additional items to be stolen from the house. The items are found in three different locations in the house, sitting out on shelves or tables. Your quest objective will update each time you obtain one of the required items. The possible items are:

- [Golden Ship Model](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Ship_Model "Skyrim:Golden Ship Model")
- [Golden Urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Urn "Skyrim:Golden Urn")
- [Jeweled Candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Candlestick "Skyrim:Jeweled Candlestick")
- [Jeweled Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Flagon "Skyrim:Jeweled Flagon")
- [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet")
- [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher")
- [Ornate Drinking Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ornate_Drinking_Horn "Skyrim:Ornate Drinking Horn")

The quest can send you to any wealthy house in the game, which amounts to 29 possible houses. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Nepos's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos%27s_House "Skyrim:Nepos's House") [Ogmund's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund%27s_House "Skyrim:Ogmund's House") [Smelter Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House") [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") | [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") [Marise Aravel's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel%27s_House "Skyrim:Marise Aravel's House") [Romlyn Dreth's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth%27s_House "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth's House") [Snow-Shod Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Manor "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor") [Valindor's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor%27s_House "Skyrim:Valindor's House") | [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") [Jala's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Jala's House") [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House") | [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") |

You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest; you also cannot kill anyone living in the house.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |

However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.

  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `MarkForDelete`, then target the golden urn, this should reveal the jeweled goblet.

(Solitude)") [Jala's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Jala's House") [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House") | [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") |

You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest; you also cannot kill anyone living in the house.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- If one of the house's occupants dies for any reason while the quest is active (even if you are not responsible), you will fail the quest.
- If you get arrested in a hold that is not where the house is located, the quest still fails.

## Bugs

- If you have already participated in the quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") it becomes impossible to enter some homes in Whiterun (the entrance to Heimskr's House is always blocked, while others should clean up after some time has passed). However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish).
  -  You can use the console command `coc`, followed by the editor id of the house.
- If you cancel a sweep quest, the items don't disappear from the house which can cause some overlap problems if the quest is assigned to that house again. If a jeweled goblet is a target and a golden urn was previously placed, the goblet will be unable to be picked up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `MarkForDelete`, then target the golden urn, this should reveal the jeweled goblet.

## Quest Stages

| The Sweep Job (TGRHC) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've been told to clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. I need to complete this job without killing any of the location's residents or getting caught and spending time in jail. *Objective 10:* Clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables (<Global=TGRHCValuablesStolen>/3) |
| 50 |  | I've cleared <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. *Objective 20:* Return the valuables to Vex |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully completed the job and received my share of the pay. |
| 250 | ☒ | By killing a resident at the task's location, I've failed this job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | During the course of this task, I was arrested and sent to the local jail. I've therefore failed the job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | Before the task could be completed, I decided to quit. I've therefore failed the job and forfeited any pay I might have received. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRHC stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGRHC`.

# Skyrim:The Sweep Job

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Nephele](/wiki/User:Nephele "User:Nephele"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Dwarfmp](/wiki/User:Dwarfmp "User:Dwarfmp"), checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Steal three specific valuable items from a wealthy house.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward) |
| ID: | TGRHC |

The Golden Urn and the Jeweled Candlestick in Evette San's House

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") about sweep jobs.
2. Enter the targeted house and steal the items she names.
3. Return them to Vex for a reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After joining the Thieves Guild, [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") will tell you that she handles all the [burglary](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job"), [shill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shill_Job "Skyrim:The Shill Job"), sweep, and [heist](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heist_Job "Skyrim:The Heist Job") jobs. Ask her for a sweep job and she will inform you that one of Skyrim's citizens has three items that the guild covets.

Steal the three items that she specifies from the provided location, and return them to Vex for a leveled gold reward. One of the three items appears in the same location as where the item for [The Burglary Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job") is placed, the only effective difference between this quest and The Burglary Job is that this quest requires two additional items to be stolen from the house. The items are found in three different locations in the house, sitting out on shelves or tables. Your quest objective will update each time you obtain one of the required items. The possible items are:

- [Golden Ship Model](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Ship_Model "Skyrim:Golden Ship Model")
- [Golden Urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Urn "Skyrim:Golden Urn")
- [Jeweled Candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Candlestick "Skyrim:Jeweled Candlestick")
- [Jeweled Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Flagon "Skyrim:Jeweled Flagon")
- [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet")
- [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher")
- [Ornate Drinking Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ornate_Drinking_Horn "Skyrim:Ornate Drinking Horn")

The quest can send you to any wealthy house in the game, which amounts to 29 possible houses. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Nepos's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos%27s_House "Skyrim:Nepos's House") [Ogmund's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund%27s_House "Skyrim:Ogmund's House") [Smelter Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House") [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") | [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") [Marise Aravel's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel%27s_House "Skyrim:Marise Aravel's House") [Romlyn Dreth's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth%27s_House "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth's House") [Snow-Shod Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Manor "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor") [Valindor's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor%27s_House "Skyrim:Valindor's House") | [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") [Jala's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Jala's House") [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House") | [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") |

You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest; you also cannot kill anyone living in the house.

However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.

  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `MarkForDelete`, then target the golden urn, this should reveal the jeweled goblet.

However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish).
  -  You can use the console command `coc`, followed by the editor id of the house.
- If you cancel a sweep quest, the items don't disappear from the house which can cause some overlap problems if the quest is assigned to that house again. If a jeweled goblet is a target and a golden urn was previously placed, the goblet will be unable to be picked up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `MarkForDelete`, then target the golden urn, this should reveal the jeweled goblet.

## Quest Stages

| The Sweep Job (TGRHC) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've been told to clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. I need to complete this job without killing any of the location's residents or getting caught and spending time in jail. *Objective 10:* Clear <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables (<Global=TGRHCValuablesStolen>/3) |
| 50 |  | I've cleared <Alias=WealthyHome> in <Alias=City> of valuables. *Objective 20:* Return the valuables to Vex |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully completed the job and received my share of the pay. |
| 250 | ☒ | By killing a resident at the task's location, I've failed this job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | During the course of this task, I was arrested and sent to the local jail. I've therefore failed the job and was forced to forfeit my share of the pay. |
| ☒ | Before the task could be completed, I decided to quit. I've therefore failed the job and forfeited any pay I might have received. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGRHC stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGRHC`.

# Skyrim:The Sweep Job

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Nephele](/wiki/User:Nephele "User:Nephele"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Dwarfmp](/wiki/User:Dwarfmp "User:Dwarfmp"), checked by [Riliane](/wiki/User:Riliane "User:Riliane") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Steal three specific valuable items from a wealthy house.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") |
| Location(s): | [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward) |
| ID: | TGRHC |

The Golden Urn and the Jeweled Candlestick in Evette San's House

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") about sweep jobs.
2. Enter the targeted house and steal the items she names.
3. Return them to Vex for a reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After joining the Thieves Guild, [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") will tell you that she handles all the [burglary](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job"), [shill](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Shill_Job "Skyrim:The Shill Job"), sweep, and [heist](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heist_Job "Skyrim:The Heist Job") jobs. Ask her for a sweep job and she will inform you that one of Skyrim's citizens has three items that the guild covets.

Steal the three items that she specifies from the provided location, and return them to Vex for a leveled gold reward. One of the three items appears in the same location as where the item for [The Burglary Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Burglary_Job "Skyrim:The Burglary Job") is placed, the only effective difference between this quest and The Burglary Job is that this quest requires two additional items to be stolen from the house. The items are found in three different locations in the house, sitting out on shelves or tables. Your quest objective will update each time you obtain one of the required items. The possible items are:

- [Golden Ship Model](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Ship_Model "Skyrim:Golden Ship Model")
- [Golden Urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Urn "Skyrim:Golden Urn")
- [Jeweled Candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Candlestick "Skyrim:Jeweled Candlestick")
- [Jeweled Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Flagon "Skyrim:Jeweled Flagon")
- [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet")
- [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher")
- [Ornate Drinking Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ornate_Drinking_Horn "Skyrim:Ornate Drinking Horn")

The quest can send you to any wealthy house in the game, which amounts to 29 possible houses. You may be assigned the same location more than once.

| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Nepos's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos%27s_House "Skyrim:Nepos's House") [Ogmund's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund%27s_House "Skyrim:Ogmund's House") [Smelter Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House") [The Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House") | [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") [Bolli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli%27s_House "Skyrim:Bolli's House") [Marise Aravel's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel%27s_House "Skyrim:Marise Aravel's House") [Romlyn Dreth's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Romlyn_Dreth%27s_House "Skyrim:Romlyn Dreth's House") [Snow-Shod Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Manor "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor") [Valindor's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Valindor%27s_House "Skyrim:Valindor's House") | [Addvar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar%27s_House "Skyrim:Addvar's House") [Bryling's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") [Evette San's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") [Jala's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Jala's House") [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House") | [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") [Carlotta Valentia's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Carlotta_Valentia%27s_House "Skyrim:Carlotta Valentia's House") [Heimskr's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr%27s_House "Skyrim:Heimskr's House") *(See [Bugs](#Bugs))* [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") [Ysolda's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_House "Skyrim:Ysolda's House") | [Atheron Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Atheron_Residence "Skyrim:Atheron Residence") [Belyn Hlaalu's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Belyn_Hlaalu%27s_House "Skyrim:Belyn Hlaalu's House") [Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") [House of Clan Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:House of Clan Cruel-Sea") [House of Clan Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:House of Clan Shatter-Shield") [Viola Giordano's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano%27s_House "Skyrim:Viola Giordano's House") |

You must not be caught and sent to jail while the quest is active, for any reason, otherwise you will fail the quest; you also cannot kill anyone living in the house.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 150 |
| 16-20 | 200 |
| 21-26 | 250 |
| 27-31 | 300 |
| 32-36 | 350 |
| 37-41 | 400 |
| 42+ | 500 |

## Notes

- If one of the house's occupants dies for any reason while the quest is active (even if you are not responsible), you will fail the quest.
- If you get arrested in a hold that is not where the house is located, the quest still fails.

## Bugs

- If you have already participated in the quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") it becomes impossible to enter some homes in Whiterun (the entrance to Heimskr's House is always blocked, while others should clean up after some time has passed). However, they can still be assigned as a possible quest destination.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - Quit the job and retake it for another location (you can load a previous save to avoid a failed quest if you wish).
  -  You can use the console command `coc`, followed by the editor id of the house.
- If you cancel a sweep quest, the items don't disappear from the house which can cause some overlap problems if the quest is assigned to that house again. If a jeweled goblet is a target and a golden urn was previously placed, the goblet will be unable to be picked up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the console command `MarkForDelete`, then target the golden urn, this should reveal the jeweled goblet.
