# Skyrim:The Taste of Death

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Daedric.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Daedric.png) | **Prepare a [feast](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") for the [Lady of Decay](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Kleppr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kleppr "Skyrim:Kleppr"), [Frabbi](/wiki/Skyrim:Frabbi "Skyrim:Frabbi"), [Brother Verulus](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus"), [Eola](/wiki/Skyrim:Eola "Skyrim:Eola") |
| Location(s): | [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn"), [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Markarth) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Markarth)"), [Reachcliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachcliff_Cave "Skyrim:Reachcliff Cave") |
| Reward: | [Ring of Namira](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Namira "Skyrim:Ring of Namira") and leveled gold (if main quest completed); [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Amulet of Arkay") (if favor quest completed) |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =3 ([Eola](/wiki/Skyrim:Eola "Skyrim:Eola")) (if main quest completed) =-2 ([Eola](/wiki/Skyrim:Eola "Skyrim:Eola")) (if Verulus dies away from the shrine, failing the main quest) =1 ([Brother Verulus](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus")) (if favor quest completed) |
| ID: | DA11Intro, DA11 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |

The dining hall in Reachcliff Cave

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Investigate the desecration of the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Markarth) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Markarth)") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").
2. Clear Reachcliff Cave of [undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr").
3. Bring a [fresh kill](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") to Namira's Shrine.
4. Do the unthinkable for your reward.

### City of Stone

*"What are you hiding, priest?"*

[Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") is the capital city of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), a place of misfortune and decay, and the denizens rarely talk to strangers about anything but the endless problems with the natives of the Reach, the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). Fortunately, the innkeeper at the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") will happily share a few local rumors when asked, so enter the tavern near the main gate and find [Kleppr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kleppr "Skyrim:Kleppr") (or [Frabbi](/wiki/Skyrim:Frabbi "Skyrim:Frabbi") if her husband is dead) behind the bar. One of the rumors may reveal problems with the local [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Markarth) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Markarth)"), which has been closed for unknown reasons. You are told to see [Brother Verulus](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") for further information, thus starting the objective that eventually leads to this quest. If Kleppr or Frabbi refuse to talk about the hall, you can find Brother Verulus yourself, who will openly tell you about current events.

Inside [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") you will witness a heated argument between Verulus and [Thongvor Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thongvor_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thongvor Silver-Blood"):

**Thongvor**: *"What are you hiding, priest?"*
**Verulus**: *"I'm not hiding anything. It's closed for a reason."*
**Thongvor**: *"Typical Imperial lies. First you take away Talos, now you're keeping us from seeing our honored dead? You and the Jarl will answer for any desecration of my ancestors' bodies."*
**Verulus**: *"That's enough, Thongvor. We're done."*

After the conversation, talk to Verulus and he will deny you access to the hall and will provide a standard explanation. You can attempt to bribe, persuade, or intimidate him, although only the first two options will get you anywhere. To succeed at bribery or persuasion, you will need to pass an easy [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech").

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| I could help if you tell me. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: All right. I was going to suggest the Jarl hire someone to sort this mess out, anyway. | | | | **Passed**: Investigate the Hall of the Dead |
| Would some coin help? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: Well, the Priesthood of Arkay always accepts generous donations. **Failed**: That's not going to work. | | | | **Passed**: Investigate the Hall of the Dead **Failed**: Nothing |
| I don't like being ignored. **(Intimidate)** | **Failed**: Then my answer is the Hall of the Dead is closed. By order of the Jarl. Understand? | | | | **Failed**: Nothing |
| I'll come back later, then. | Arkay keep you and protect you. | | | | Nothing |

He will then explain the macabre situation in the hall and reveal the truth: *"We've discovered that some of the dead have been... eaten. Flesh has been chewed off, bones were snapped to get at the marrow inside."* Verulus then proceeds to ask you to investigate the Hall of the Dead and hands you the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Hall_of_the_Dead_Key "Skyrim:Markarth Hall of the Dead Key") to the hall. This is the beginning of the favor quest.

Alternatively, you can completely ignore Verulus and pick the lock to the hall. Entering the hall this way will trigger the main quest; however, unless you persuade or bribe him, you will not be able to befriend him using the favor quest.

### Hall of the Dead

Eola in the Hall of the Dead

Moments after entering, a female voice will echo through the hall, saying, *"Not many would walk blindly into a crypt, smelling of steel and blood, but not fear. I feel the hunger inside of you. Gnawing at you. You see the dead and your mouth grows wet. Your stomach growls. It's all right. I will not shun you for what you are. Stay. I will tell you everything you have forgotten."* After the speech, [Eola](/wiki/Skyrim:Eola "Skyrim:Eola") will then run up to you and continue in the same vein, trying to seduce you with suggestions and accusations. When she is finished, three options are available. If you choose the third option, the quest will immediately fail, as she will attack you, with no option to yield. You can still complete the favor quest and receive your [reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Amulet of Arkay") from Verulus, but will never get to experience The Taste of Death.

If you instead pick any of the two other options, Eola will continue her seductive behavior, eventually mentioning the Lady of Decay, [Namira](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira"), and a so-called safe haven for cannibals like yourself. Regardless of your answer, the quest will start. If you ask her about the place, she will mark [Reachcliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachcliff_Cave "Skyrim:Reachcliff Cave") on your map and reveal the truth about the desecration of the hall. Recently, the cave itself saw the dead rise from their graves, forcing Eola to flee and live in the hall and feast on its more passive inhabitants. She will task you with clearing the cave, and will then cast her [invisibility spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_(spell) "Skyrim:Invisibility (spell)"), asking you to meet her at the cave entrance. She will also assure you that the hall will see no further disturbances, and will then leave. Go talk to Brother Verulus and tell him the good news. He will be quite happy, hand you his [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Amulet of Arkay") as a reward and return to his duties inside the hall. This completes the favor quest.

### Cave of the Dead

*"Bring Verulus here. The Lady of Decay will do the rest."*

Reachcliff Cave is located east and slightly south of Markarth and can easily be reached by crossing the bridge to the south from [Karthspire](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire "Skyrim:Karthspire"). As promised, Eola will be waiting for you near the entrance and will seek you out as you approach. She will reveal that the opposition inside the cave consists of [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") enemies and the whole cave has to be cleared. You can choose to have her as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), so decide whether or not to accept her offer and head inside. Watch out for the higher-leveled draugr in the second chamber and carefully proceed forward. Eola is a powerful follower and will not hesitate to [summon](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") a [flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach") or revive defeated draugr for extra help. In the catacombs, take a left for a difficult jump to a chest on a small ledge. (Use Whirlwind Sprint for an effortless little zoom across the gap). After a short trek, you will arrive in a room with several draugr, including the boss, so dispose of them all and take a look around; the chamber consists of a huge dinner table, and, in the southern end, the very altar of Namira. Eola will now approach and thank you for reclaiming the Shrine, and will ask you to bring in a fresh kill for your initiation into the coven, specifically a priest filled with the taste of the easy life, [Brother Verulus](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus"). She will then hand you 100 gold to cover expenses and show you the way out. A shortcut to the outside world will now have opened in the room next to the Shrine, so exit the cave and travel to Markarth.

### Champion of Namira

Back in the Hall of the Dead, the unsuspecting priest has picked up his daily routines and spends most of his time sweeping or praying near the Shrine of Arkay, convinced that everything is all right. Talk to him and ask him for assistance during your travels. In order to get him to follow, you need to pass a speech check. As with the initial conversation with him about investigating the hall, only the first two options will get you anywhere. (However, persuading may be impossible, necessitating a bribe—see [Bugs](#Bugs).)

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| There would be treasure to share... **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Treasure, you say? I suppose the Jarl won't mind if I'm gone for a little while. Lead on. **Failed**: You know, in the Priesthood of Arkay, we have a joke about an empty pocket being better than a full grave. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Namira's Shrine **Failed**: Nothing |
| I'm willing to pay. **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: That's no small amount of coin, friend. I suppose I can come with you for a short venture. Lead on. **Failed**: I'm just not up for it, sorry. I'd rather stay here, have a glass of wine, and perform my rites to Arkay in peace. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Namira's Shrine **Failed**: Nothing |
| You're coming with me. Now. **(Intimidate)** | **Failed**: I think you need to calm down before I summon the guards. | | | | **Failed**: Nothing |
| Never mind, then. | Arkay watch over you. | | | | Nothing |

Leave the Hall of the Dead and fast travel to the secret back entrance to Reachcliff Cave. When you enter the dining hall, you will find several well-known Markarth citizens seated at the large table, all hungry and ready for the evening feast: [Lisbet](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet "Skyrim:Lisbet"), [Banning](/wiki/Skyrim:Banning "Skyrim:Banning"), [Hogni Red-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hogni_Red-Arm "Skyrim:Hogni Red-Arm"), [Sanyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanyon "Skyrim:Sanyon"), and [Nimphaneth](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimphaneth "Skyrim:Nimphaneth"). The table will be set with beverages, bread, cheese and two pieces of [human flesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Flesh "Skyrim:Human Flesh"). A confused Brother Verulus will approach the table, stuttering. Eola will immediately be over him and will use her seductive charms to make him forget where he is and feel incredibly tired. She will then proceed to invite him to take a rest on the altar in front of the Shrine of Namira, something he will do right away. Listening to the guests' private conversations makes it quite clear what they're all waiting for: the flesh of Verulus. Head to the altar where Eola will invite you to start carving the sleeping priest in front of you.

Death of a priest

At this point, you can choose to kill Eola, which will net you a leveled amount of gold from a grateful Brother Verulus and a fight against all the dinner guests, including the quest-related Lisbet, dog seller Banning and Markarth market merchant Hogni Red-Arm. Killing Eola will cause the quest to fail.

Slay the sleeping priest in cold blood, which will make an excited Eola invite you to have the very first bite. Examine the dead priest and choose the option 'eat'. You will then be treated to an animation of yourself feasting on the still warm body of Verulus, and Namira will finally speak to you from her realm. *"Mortal. I am Namira, the Lady of Decay. Your consumption of the blood and bile of Arkay's own is pleasing to me. I give you my ring. Wear it, and when you feast on the flesh of the dead I will grant you my power."* You will then receive the [Ring of Namira](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Namira "Skyrim:Ring of Namira") which increases your stamina by 50 points and allows you to feed on corpses for increased health and health regeneration of 50 points for 5 minutes. Eola will then welcome you to the coven and will be available as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") should you ever need her. When all is said and done, leave the cannibals to their feast and head out into Skyrim.

#### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

## Notes

- If Thongvor is Jarl of Markarth before you enter Understone Keep for the first time, the argument between him and Verulus does not happen. This can happen if you have completed [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") or the Civil War quests (and sided with the Stormcloaks) before coming to Understone Keep. There is no change in Verulus' dialogue if you speak to him in this case.
- After Verulus agrees to follow you to the cave, he will become a follower and will follow you anywhere until you enter the cave. Unlike nearly all other quest followers, if you already have a follower when he joins you, he won't replace them.
- Though Namira makes no visible appearance, she's voiced by an unseen NPC named [Voice of Namira](/wiki/Skyrim:Voice_of_Namira "Skyrim:Voice of Namira") located in an unreachable room east of Namira's shrine.
- If you decide to save Brother Verulus, you can use a Calm spell on the other dinner guests after killing Eola to end the quest, but Banning and Hogni Red-Arm will never leave the feast to return to Markarth. Lisbet will return to her store, but she and Imedhnain will be hostile towards you. Use another calm spell on them and leave the shop. Wait at least a day before returning and Lisbet will be friendly again, acting as though the feast had been successful.
- If you are a werewolf and have decided to save Brother Verulus by killing cannibals, be careful when you go in to beast form as it can cause issues. If you go into beast form, Verulus may wake up early in the middle of the fight and start the conversation with you as if he has already been saved. You will receive the same reward from him, but he may get killed or possibly stuck walking out the door and be unable to return to Markarth. If he sees you in beast form after the fight is over and has already paid you, he will attack you.
- After killing Brother Verulus in Reachcliff Cave, you are able to search his body and get back your earlier bribe.
- After completing the quest you can speak to the other guests, many of whom you might recognize from [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). If you meet the guests later, while they are at work, you can ask about the feast to which they will respond *"Only the guests must know."* You may also encounter [Sigar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigar "Skyrim:Sigar") in the wilderness, feasting on a fresh corpse.
- If you attack any guest after completing the quest, Eola becomes aggressive. Killing Eola, even after quest completion, causes your journal to show all quest objectives as failed, although you will retain the Ring if you had received it.
- If you are wearing the Ring of Namira and receive the Cursed Ring of Hircine from Sinding during the quest [Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight"), you will forever be able to feed off of bodies and obtain +50 health and +50% health regeneration.

## Bugs

- If you enter the Hall of the Dead too quickly after speaking with Verulus, he may follow you in and react as though you were trespassing.
- If you run through the Hall of the Dead and exit the door on the other side before Eola has finished her speech, then re-enter the hall, she will pick up where she left off but a new instance of the same speech will begin upon entry, causing an echo like effect. Eola will then run up to you twice, and vanish once only to return again repeating her opening dialogue several times. The quest progress appears unaffected by this glitch. **?**
- If Eola dies sooner than intended, Brother Verulus may become glitched and will continually approach you for conversation whenever you enter the keep.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- If you have the miscellaneous objective to inform Verulus that you've cleared out the Hall of the Dead, be sure to speak to him about this first. Failure to do so can lead to him glitching and not following you.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- Verulus cannot be persuaded to follow the player to the cave without a bribe (or the [Amulet of Articulation](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Articulation "Skyrim:Amulet of Articulation")), because the Speech check is done to Verulus instead of the player.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=18667))
- If Eola is told to wait outside Reachcliff Cave, she will continually forcegreet.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, addresses this issue. This is due to a missing stage to block this from happening.
- If you have Dawnguard installed, the game may crash every time you get near Reachcliff Cave.
  -  You can use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `player.moveto` to teleport in and out of the cave.
- Verulus may not be able to enter through the secret entrance, instead trying to take the long way around.
  -  You can use the console command `player.moveto` to teleport yourself to him.
- If Eola somehow dies in Reachcliff Cave, the quest will end. Your target will no longer be there and the quest will disappear from your journal. There is no trace of you ever having the quest.
- The shortcut exit from the chamber next to the shrine in Reachcliff Cave may fail to open, requiring you to take the long way out. However, the shortcut may be open if you exit the cave via the main entrance and reenter it through the secret entrance.
- After Verulus has been killed, the option will still show to search him. Attempting to search him will present you with the "Leave." or "Eat." options. Choosing "Eat." will not show you feeding on Verulus, but the quest will continue anyway.
  -  If you scroll out into 3rd-person, the animation will show as it should.
- If the quest was initiated by speaking to Verulus, do not ask Kleppr or Frabbi if they have heard any rumors until Verulus has been informed the Hall of the Dead is safe, or "Speak to Brother Verulus about the Hall of the Dead" will be stuck in the Miscellaneous quest category.
  -  You can use the console command `setstage da11intro 20` to clear the quest.
- After killing Verulus on the Altar of Namira, he may clip through the table so it is impossible to feast on him. **?**
  - Saving the game and reloading will fix this.
  - You can also use the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout to get the body out from inside the table.
  -  You can use the console command `tcl` to clip through the floor and reach his body.
- You may not be able to find Verulus and therefore cannot complete the quest. **?**
- If Eola is asked to wait outside Reachcliff Cave, she will continually forcegreet the player.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- If you initiate the quest with Eola, and then subsequently kill her, failing the quest, you may still be able to speak to the guests about seeing them at the feast, despite never having been there.
- Eola may become stuck in a location while in combat mode. **?**
  - Casting [Calm](/wiki/Skyrim:Calm "Skyrim:Calm") to bring her out of combat mode fixes this.
- After finishing the quest, Lisbet and the others may be stuck in Reachcliff Cave.
  - Telling Eola to follow you and walking back to Markarth should fix this issue.

## Quest Stages

| Investigate the Hall of the Dead (DA11Intro) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | *Objective 5:* Speak to Verulus about the Hall of the Dead |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Investigate the Hall of the Dead |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Tell Verulus the Hall of the dead is safe |
| 20 | ☑ |  |
| 200 | ☑ |  |
| The Taste of Death (DA11) | | |
| 10 |  | Eola in Markarth wants me to join her in worshipping Namira, the Lady of Decay, by feasting on the flesh of the dead. She has something planned inside Reachcliff Cave. *Objective 10:* Clear the Draugr from Reachcliff Cave |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Speak to Eola |
| 30 |  | Eola wants me to lure Brother Verulus to the Shrine of Namira, so that her coven of cannibals can feast on his flesh. *Objective 30:* Convince Verulus to follow you |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Lead Verulus to the Shrine of Namira |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Kill Verulus |
| 60 |  | Brother Verulus is dead, and I've been asked to feast on his dead body to complete my initiation into Namira's coven. *Objective 60:* Feast on Verulus |
| 100 | ☑ | I have feasted on the body of Brother Verulus and have been rewarded with Namira's Ring. |
| 250 | ☒ | I killed Eola. Whatever she could have offered me was lost when she died. |
| 500 | ☒ | I killed Brother Verulus outside of the shrine of Namira's presence. The cannabilistic ritual to gain Namira's blessing has failed. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table:
  - DA11Intro: 0, 12.
  - DA11: 0, 5, 15, 45, 70, 200, 225, 600.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DA11 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DA11`.

# Skyrim:The Temple of Miraak

## Overview

[Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak").
2. Find and talk to [Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea").
3. Enter the temple and travel through it.
4. Read the Black Book *[Waking Dreams](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Waking_Dreams_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Waking Dreams (book)")* at the end of the temple.

### Here in His Temple

When you reach the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") you will find that the exterior is under construction by the enthralled people of Solstheim, all of them forced by [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)") to rebuild the temple. You may also notice that you are not the only unenslaved person around, as [Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") resident, [Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea"), will be attempting to contact the mindless builders. Enter the center of the structure and the quest will begin with Frea seeking you out. She explains that she is there to either free or avenge her people, revealing that the workers are from [her village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). She is also knowledgeable about the return of Miraak and will offer you companionship to help defeat him. Her assistance starts with locating the entrance to the underground Temple. Soon afterward, a gate will open and two [cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Cultist "Skyrim:Cultist") will come rushing out, revealing the entrance. Dispose of them and follow Frea into the temple.

### Temple of Miraak

[Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea") waits until the path is clear.

Go through the first corridor and check the neighboring rooms for a few healing potions and a chest with minor loot. Proceed north until you reach a room with a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers [darts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"). Two cultists will attack as well, but Frea will quickly show that she is a capable warrior and kill them on the spot. There is a restless [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") in the upright sarcophagus on the left-hand raised section in this room. There is also a dead (lootable) [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") in the sarcophagus on the right-hand side. These do not seem to emerge unless you climb onto the relevant raised section of floor. More pressure plates can be found in the next room, both of them triggering [battering rams](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram"). Avoid them and head west. Pull the lever to open the gate into what appears to be a torture-showroom, with several skeletons in cages and a throne that provides a good view of the mayhem. Frea will spot something near the throne but reckons it's impossible to reach. The task is of course left to you. Next to the broken stairs, jump onto the overturned pillar and from there, jump down to the platform and the throne. Claim the contents from the boss-leveled chest and jump back down. As you approach the bloody steps underneath the cages, a boss-leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") will break out of his sarcophagus and attack. When walking down the stairs, more cultists will show up. Finish the fights and continue forward. Activate the handle to gain access to the northeastern tunnel and fight the draugr who resides there. When you reach another pressure plate and a [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") trap, you will be attacked on all sides by leveled draugr. The path now splits, but both paths will land you in the same catacombs with quick access to a huge chamber protected by yet another pressure plate triggering [flame spouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap"). In the chamber, quite a few swinging blades will activate. Frea will order you to solve the problem, and even make herself comfortable while she waits. The blades' area of effect is easily avoided by simply hugging the walls of the chamber, though you can also just dodge them, by waiting for a second of space to pass through unarmed quickly, or by using the shouts; [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal"), or [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"). Stop the traps by activating the handle on the other side of the room and Frea will come walking up to you. Head through the door with her and face a closed iron gate. The adjacent window reveals a handle, so make your way there and activate it. There is also a chain in the room behind the gate that reveals a chamber with a chest. Behind the gate is another huge chamber, and several raised wooden bridges will fall into place when you enter. Two leveled draugr and a cultist will be waiting to the south. Dispose of them all and enter the [Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak_Sanctum "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak Sanctum").

### Sanctum

The Gatekeeper attacks.

The path ahead is quite narrow and leads onto a bridge where you will encounter at least six [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). Next up are several draugr bursting out of their coffins, along with more pressure plates triggering battering rams. You will now be in the chamber you just crossed on the bridge. To the right is a passage leading to a room with several potions, coin purses, and two spell tomes: an apprentice level [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") and an apprentice level [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell tome. Take what you want and return to the huge room where you will encounter more draugr and cultists. Head around the pit in the center of the room and go west. Before long, you will hear the easily recognizable chant from a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") in the room ahead. The room contains both the word wall and a provocative trophy, hung there by Miraak as a symbol of his superiority. While Frea comments on this, go and learn the first word for the [Dragon Aspect](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Aspect "Skyrim:Dragon Aspect") shout (or the second, if you have already learned the first word in Raven Rock Mine). This will cause numerous draugr to attack, including the unique [Gatekeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Gatekeeper "Skyrim:Gatekeeper"). After the battle, search the Gatekeeper for the [temple key](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak_Key "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak Key") then find his sarcophagus on the western wall and unlock the door behind it. It opens to a macabre dining table, the skeletal guests still in their seats. Behind the table is a tunnel leading to a larger dining area with a kitchen behind. When you reach the kitchen, Frea will realize it is a dead end and will order you to have a look around while she backtracks to the dining area.

The kitchen contains an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), a few potions and ingredients, and most importantly, a path in the southeastern corner leading to a handle. When activated, a hidden door in the dining area will open up. In the next chamber, Frea will hint that there may be something in there that fills in the holes in the story of [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)"), and will head into the next room and gaze at the statues. Similar to her actions back in the trapped room, she will ask you to activate the button while she waits at a safe distance. The handle removes the grate in the floor and reveals a wooden staircase going down. Head down and follow the path to another set of stairs. Proceed through two empty rooms until you find a handle lowering the rock wall. Continue down yet more stairs and open the door. A huge chamber will be revealed, guarded by draugr and skeletons, and booby-trapped with [tripwires](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") triggering [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders"). Make your way to the top and face a boss-leveled draugr, being sure to loot the chest behind his sarcophagus. Activate the chain on the southern wall and follow the serpentine path until you reach your target, a pedestal holding a [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book (book)"), *[Waking Dreams](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Waking_Dreams_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Waking Dreams (book)")*.

### Waking Dreams

*"Who are you to dare set foot here?"*

When you read the Black Book, dark tentacles will reach out of the book's pages and grab you. You will be transported to a [strange realm](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(Waking_Dreams) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (Waking Dreams)") just in time to see [a dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahrotaar "Skyrim:Sahrotaar") arrive. Nearby are a few [seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") standing guard and Miraak himself. You will be unable to move and can do nothing but listen to Miraak's monologue: *"Who are you to dare set foot here? Ahh... You are Dragonborn. I can feel it. And yet..."* At this point his dialogue will differ depending on your progress of the main quest (see [notes](#Notes)). After the conditional comment he will continue, *"You have no idea of the true power a Dragonborn can wield!"* He will then demonstrate the Dragon Aspect shout. *"Mul... Qah Diiv! This realm is beyond you. You have no power here. And it is only a matter of time before Solstheim is also mine. I already control the minds of its people. Soon they will finish building my temple, and I can return home."* He will then turn to the four seekers and say: *"Send him/her back where he/she came from. He/She can await my arrival with the rest of Tamriel."* The seekers will then shower you with magic and while you slowly lose consciousness, you can see Miraak mount the dragon and fly away. Moments later, you will be back in the [Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak_Sanctum "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak Sanctum") and Frea will demand an explanation. As soon as she realizes the potential danger of the situation, she will suggest that you follow her to her village and talk to her father, [Storn Crag-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider"). This ends the quest and begins the next in line, [The Fate of the Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fate_of_the_Skaal "Skyrim:The Fate of the Skaal").

Since the Black Book is an inventory item, you may re-read it at any time, and explore it more thoroughly in Miraak's absence, all the way up to getting the second (or third) word of the Dragon Aspect shout: however you will not be able to unlock the final part of the book until the concluding part of the Main Quest, when you \*must\* return here.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **The Temple of Miraak** (20 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- During your encounter with Miraak his dialogue will differ, based on your progress and how many dragons you have killed. This table shows the dialogue bits and the conditions:

:   | Dialogue | Conditions |
    | --- | --- |
    | *"You have done little beyond killing a few dragons."* | Fewer than 10 dragons killed |
    | *"You have defeated dragons, yes, but still..."* | Between 10 and 25 dragons killed |
    | *"You have slain a great many dragons, I see. And yet..."* | Over 25 dragons killed |
    | *"So you have slain Alduin... Well done. I could have slain him myself, back when I walked the earth, but I chose a different path."* | Completed [Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer") |

- When you kill the very first dragon after completing this quest, Miraak will appear and steal the soul from you, as he will 25% of the time with other dragons you kill until the Dragonborn questline is completed. His appearances are scripted, and will occur regardless of if you are in Skyrim or on Solstheim. He is unable to be attacked or interacted with, as he will appear in an ethereal state and is a "ghost". The only option when encountering him is to just let him steal the soul from you. His first appearance is *always* guaranteed; afterwards he will only appear 25% of the time. There is one exception in some cases for the first dragon you kill; see the notes of the next quest for details.

- This quest may be started after completing [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") by cleansing the [Wind Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_Stone "Skyrim:Wind Stone"), Talking to Storn afterwards will have him direct you to the temple, starting this quest and bypassing Dragonborn (quest) entirely.

## Bugs

- Frea may randomly appear at locations throughout the temple, and may not follow you once the next quest has begun. If you dismiss your follower, or tell them to wait outside, and re-enter the temple, she should reappear near where you found the book. This seems to happen because the script that causes her to lead you out on the next quest only activates if you speak to her near that spot.
- If you exit the temple before finishing your search, Frea's script will believe you left and therefore walk back to the entrance interior and will not follow you until you rejoin her there and pull out your weapons. She will then re-follow you back down and behave normally. **?**
- After reading the Black Book and being teleported to Apocrypha, Miraak may be cut off after the first line "The time comes soon when..." and you then are transported back to the Sanctum unable to move indefinitely. This can be fixed by saving in Apocrypha and then loading afterwards.
- After reading the Black Book, completing the dialogue, and leaving, Frea will say her lines and walk back to Skaal Village but will never talk to Storn and the next quest will not begin.
- The variable Miraak checks when determining how many dragons you have slain is never updated by the game, resulting in him always saying, *"You have done little beyond killing a few dragons."* unless you have slain Alduin.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.2, addresses this issue. The dialogue is instead determined by how many dragon souls you have absorbed.
- Miraak's scene (DLC2MQ02MiraakApocryphaScene) has an incorrect gender check which blocks the response line for female player characters.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug.
- Frea can be asked what the Tree Stone is. Unfortunately, there is an unnecessary restriction on the topic preventing it from being accessible in an interior.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| The Temple of Miraak (DLC2MQ02) | | |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 22, 50.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2MQ02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2MQ02`.

# Skyrim:The Throat of the World

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Main.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Main.png) | **Receive a lesson from [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") |
| Location(s): | [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar"), [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World") |
| Reward: | One unlocked word of power for the [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath") shout and the whole [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies") shout |
| ID: | MQ204 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall") | **Next →** [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge") [Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial") (finish [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)") first) | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall") | | → Next | [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge") [Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial") (finish [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)") first) | | |

Paarthurnax

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
2. Learn the Word of Power from Paarthurnax.
3. Use your "[Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath")" [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") on Paarthurnax.
4. Talk to Paarthurnax.

### Dragonrend

Learning the Clear Skies shout

With the information about [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin")'s defeat learned at Sky Haven Temple, travel to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar") to meet with the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards").

When you arrive, you will first need to turn over the [Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:Horn of Jurgen Windcaller") and learn the final Word for [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") [if you have not yet done so](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller"). Once you have, tell [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir") that you need to learn the [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") used to defeat Alduin. He will be quite shocked and ask where you learned about such a shout. While the Greybeards and the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") do not have a history of cooperation, if you refuse to tell Arngeir where you came across the information, he will not help you. You can either tell him that you learned it from [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall") or that you were talking to the Blades. In either case, he will be strongly offended and will be reluctant to help. Depending on your response, [Einarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Einarth "Skyrim:Einarth") may chastise Arngeir for his impertinence by saying, *"Arngeir. Rek/Rok los Dovahkiin, Strundu'ul. Rek/Rok fen tinvaak [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)")."* meaning, *"Arngeir. She/He is Dovahkiin, Stormcrown. She/He will speak (with) Paarthurnax"*.

Regardless, Arngeir eventually offers a hasty apology, saying the decision to help or not help you is not ultimately his. He tells you that the shout used to end Alduin's reign of terror is called [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend"). However, Arngeir cannot teach it to you because he does not know it and the origins have been lost. If asked, Arngeir will explain that the shout was created during the terrifying reign of the dragons and is a shout of pure evil, embodying all the cruelty, fear, and horror of the time. If you want to learn this shout, you must speak with Paarthurnax, the leader of their order. Further questioning reveals that Paarthurnax lives in seclusion at the peak of the Throat of the World and surpasses all of the Greybeards in the [Way of the Voice](/wiki/Lore:Way_of_the_Voice "Lore:Way of the Voice").

Arngeir will offer to help you reach Paarthurnax and leads you out into the courtyard where you will be taught all three words of the shout [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies"). You are now ready to attempt the trek up to the summit of the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World"). The path up is blocked by [magical winds](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Magical_Wind "Skyrim:Traps") dealing severe [frost damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage"), even with [resist frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Frost "Skyrim:Resist Frost") effects. Use the shout Arngeir gave you to clear away the damaging mists.

### Paarthurnax

When you reach the summit, a dragon approaches. However, resist the urge to attack, as the dragon will land and address you: *"Drem Yol Lok. Greetings, wunduniik. I am Paarthurnax. Who are you? What brings you to my strunmah ... my mountain?"* After you explain your objective, Paarthurnax will respond: *"Drem. Patience. There are formalities that must be observed, at the first meeting of two of the dov. By long tradition, the elder speaks first. Hear my Thu'um! Feel it in your bones. Match it, if you are [Dovahkiin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dovahkiin "Skyrim:Dovahkiin")!"* He will then shoot a bout of flame onto a wall and encourage you to participate in "tinvaak" (loosely translated, "conversation").

Inspect the word he left behind to learn a new Shout, and Paarthurnax will grant you his knowledge of it, saying *"A gift, Dovahkiin. Yol. Understand Fire as the dov do. Now, show me what you can do. Greet me not as mortal, but as dovah!"* Use this new shout on Paarthurnax. He will agree with the opinions voiced by Greybeards that "the dragonblood runs strong in you", even if you are a "joor" (mortal), and offer to answer your questions.

After the formalities, ask Paarthurnax about [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend"). He will admit that he was expecting this, as "Alduin and Dovahkiin return together". Though he doesn't know the shout, he believes it could be learned by returning to the beginning of the "Tiid-Ahraan", the Time-Wound on the Throat of the World. An [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Lore:Elder_Scrolls "Lore:Elder Scrolls"), or "Kel" is needed to activate the portal and allow you to view the first Tongues using the Thu'um to defeat Alduin. As the quest ends, the dragon admits he has no idea where to find an Elder Scroll. Your quest log suggests you talk to Arngeir or [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") for more information.

## Notes

- If you have already acquired an Elder Scroll by completing the [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane") quest, Paarthurnax urges you to the Time-Wound, and the quest [Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane") will begin immediately.
- You can use the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout to stroll through the mists except for the first cloud; passage through it requires [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies").
- If you unlock the word yourself at just the right time, before Paarthurnax gives you his "understanding", he will teach you the second word for Fire Breath instead of the first (or the third if you started out knowing the second).
- Paarthurnax will say that he is teaching you Yol, no matter which Word the wall actually teaches you.
- You can climb to the very top without going through the temple and the barriers, though Paarthurnax will not be present.
- [Viinturuth](/wiki/Skyrim:Viinturuth "Skyrim:Viinturuth") will be resurrected by [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") once this quest is completed, at the [mound](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds") northwest of [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill") and near [Lake Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Yorgrim "Skyrim:Lake Yorgrim").

- Choose the optional dialogue and say you want to learn about:

:   | Word | Translation | Effect Name | Description | Notes |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Fus | force | [Force Without Effort](/wiki/Skyrim:Force_Without_Effort "Skyrim:Force Without Effort") | You stagger 25% less and foes stagger 25% more. | Augments power attacks and [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout. |
    | Feim | fade | [Eternal Spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Eternal_Spirit "Skyrim:Eternal Spirit") | While Ethereal, you recover health 25% faster. | Only active and visible on Active Effects menu when using [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout. |
    | Yol | fire | [The Fire Within](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fire_Within "Skyrim:The Fire Within") | [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath") shout deals 25% more damage. |  |

:   These increase the respective shout capabilities. You can only have one active at a time.

## Bugs

- You may be unable to learn the [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies") shout.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
  - Reloading a save from before talking to [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir") then following him outside immediately will usually fix the problem. Sometimes you need to watch him whisper to words on the ground to ensure they stay lit.
- If you leave before shouting Fire Breath, your shouts' cooldowns will recharge completely every few seconds. This exploit allows you to use powerful shouts very frequently, which will have an unbalancing effect on the game.
- As you talk to Paarthurnax, he may fly up high, above the mountain, and begin circling. You may continue your conversation, though you cannot hear him, so it is advised you turn subtitles on. This does not otherwise impede the progress of the quest.
- The word wall may not activate properly. If you come back later, the word may be highlighted, but you can no longer learn the word from it.
  -  In the [Console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), enter `teachword 20e17` to unlock the first word. If you already have one or two words of Fire Breath, use `20e18` or `20e19`, respectively.

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQ204 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQ204`.

# Skyrim:The Tower Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Doomstone.png) | Standing Stone: The Tower Stone ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Tower+Stone)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DoomstoneSnowy01 | |
| Region | |
| [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | |
| Location | |
| About halfway between [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), on a high cliff. | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Quicksilver](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore") | 2 |

The Tower Stone

**The Tower Stone** is one of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim.

The Tower Stone can be found about halfway between [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), on a high snow-covered cliff, north-northeast of [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave").

Its description reads: *"Once a day, those under the sign of The Tower have the option to automatically open an Expert or lower lock."*

## The Tower Stone

.jpg)

The Tower Stone, when activated

It is found high on a glacier or cliff, the only approaches are from the east or southeast. The stone is standing at the top of a flight of stairs facing due west. There is a birds' nest in a bush overhanging the edge to the right of the stairs with a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") inside. There is also another birds' nest overhanging the edge behind the stone, although beware as getting back can be risky. To the left of the stairs is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush among some rubble.

## Notes

- Locks opened using the Tower Stone will not count toward "Locks Picked" in the Stats screen, and will not count toward the Thief achievement.
- You can use the Stone's blessing to your advantage as a way to escape from prison, as both chests should have Expert locks. Simply retrieve your equipment (including your lockpicks) from one chest and unlock the other one.
- On top of the adjacent glacier to the north is a skeleton resting beside an unlocked chest and a copy of the heavy armor skill book [The Knights of the Nine](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Knights_of_the_Nine "Skyrim:The Knights of the Nine").
- Two [quicksilver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore") veins are located 220 ft east of the stone.
- If you approach the Stone from underneath by the shoreline, you will not be able to discover it. This may also make it seem as if the marker is placed in the wrong place.

## Bugs

- There is no loading screen for the Tower Stone.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:The Treasury House

## Overview

The Treasury House

**The Treasury House** is the main financial institution for [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") and [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"). It is on the first terrace above and in the northern area of the city. It provides financial support and services for the landowners of the Reach, notably the Silver-Blood family and its patrons. All the miners, farmers, and day-laborers of the Reach get their wages through the Treasury House. [Rhiada](/wiki/Skyrim:Rhiada "Skyrim:Rhiada") runs the front desk, where the actual treasury is kept behind an expert-locked gate. [Nana Ildene](/wiki/Skyrim:Nana_Ildene "Skyrim:Nana Ildene") (who has worked there for over twenty years) and [Donnel](/wiki/Skyrim:Donnel "Skyrim:Donnel") keep things tidy. [Thonar Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood"), who handles all of his family's business, effectively controls the establishment. [Betrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Betrid_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Betrid Silver-Blood"), Thonar's wife and an admitted and unrepentant gold-digger, can also be found here.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Betrid Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Betrid_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Betrid Silver-Blood")\*  [Donnel](/wiki/Skyrim:Donnel "Skyrim:Donnel")\*  [Nana Ildene](/wiki/Skyrim:Nana_Ildene "Skyrim:Nana Ildene")\*  [Reburrus Quintilius](/wiki/Skyrim:Reburrus_Quintilius "Skyrim:Reburrus Quintilius")\*\*  [Rhiada](/wiki/Skyrim:Rhiada "Skyrim:Rhiada")  [Thonar Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood")\*\*\*  [Thongvor Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thongvor_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thongvor Silver-Blood")\*\*  [Yngvar the Singer](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvar_the_Singer "Skyrim:Yngvar the Singer")\*\* |

\* These people die during [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy").
\*\* These persons will be no longer available in this house, which can only happen through doing the quest Season Unending, and then progressing through the Civil War on the Imperial side.
\*\*\* Dies after completing [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine") in favor of Madanach.

## Related Quests

- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

## The Treasury House

It is a large building, like all in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") is built into the hillside. From the entrance there is a short corridor to the main room with a large counter in front of you and raised areas in the southeastern and southwestern corners. There are stairs along the east and west wall leading to [Thonar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood")'s quarters and a pair of twin bedrooms used by the employees. By the bottom of the stairs are stone tables and chairs, with numerous [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and sacks around the building. Most of the cookware in the building is high quality, including [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), [jugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug"), [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), etc. [Rhiada](/wiki/Skyrim:Rhiada "Skyrim:Rhiada") will be stood behind the counter and make you unwelcome with comments about it only being for the employees of the Silver-Blood family.

Inside the Treasury House

On the counter is a wooden bowl containing a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flower, two [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") on a wooden plate, a bowl containing a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and a plate with two more dragon's tongue flowers on it. While under the counter is a collection of cookware, a bunch of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") and a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"). to the rear of the counter is a flight of stairs up to an expert-locked gate concealing an expert-locked [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Safe "Skyrim:Safe") with three [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot") on each side of it.

On the raised section in the southeast corner is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on a barrel, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") on a crate and a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") on the floor. The table by the stairs holds the same as the other one, except it has a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") instead of alto wine. At the top of the stairs is a junction with a twin bedroom to the east and west. The one to the west consists of two owned single beds, one against a ledge to the south and the other against a ledge to the north. On the first ledge is a bottle of wine, a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), two red and a green apple, while on the second ledge is a copy of *[Scourge of the Gray Quarter](/wiki/Skyrim:Scourge_of_the_Gray_Quarter "Skyrim:Scourge of the Gray Quarter")* and a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"). Against the west wall is a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and with a piece of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") and bottle of alto wine on top. The bedroom to the east consists of another two owned single beds, one against a ledge to the north and the other against a ledge to the south. The ledge to the north has a copy of *[Nords Arise!](/wiki/Skyrim:Nords_Arise! "Skyrim:Nords Arise!")*, a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and two loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on top and the ledge to the south has two bottles of Nord mead on top. To the east is a tall wardrobe with a bottle of wine and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") on a crate to the right.

By the raised section to the southwest is a kettle containing two cabbages and a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), while on the raised section is a round wooden table with a bottle of alto wine and a bottle of wine on top. Along the west wall is a dresser, with a small coin purse on a barrel to the right and further right is a stone ledge with a red apple in front of a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Vernaccus and Bourlor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vernaccus_and_Bourlor "Skyrim:Vernaccus and Bourlor")*. The stone table by these stairs has two wooden chairs and has a bottle of alto wine, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a red apple, a loaf of bread and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") on top. [Betrid Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Betrid_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Betrid Silver-Blood") spend all her time sat at this table. In the northwest corner, up the stairs is the door to Thonar's quarters which is apprentice-locked.

His quarters consist of two rooms, the first has a central stone table with two chairs. It is laid with plenty of cookware as well as a bottle of wine, a baked potato, two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a rack of [dog meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog_Meat "Skyrim:Dog Meat"), three loaves of bread and several pieces of cheese. There is an alcove to the west with an owned single bed in against the west wall with a ledge running along the wall holding a copy of *[The Cake and The Diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cake_and_The_Diamond "Skyrim:The Cake and The Diamond")*. To the left of the alcove is a set of shelves holding two loaves of bread, a cabbage, a potato in a cast iron pot and several pieces of cheese, while to the right of the alcove is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot. Against the east wall is a large fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a pot containing a cabbage and a wooden bowl containing two red and a green apple on either side. To the left of the fireplace is a food barrel with a goat cheese wedge on top and a basket on the floor containing a gourd and two cabbages, with a rack hanging from the ceiling above it holding a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a garlic braid and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam").

To the north is a doorway into a small bedroom most of which is taken up with a large double bed coming out from the north wall. To the right of the bed, on a stone ledge is an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") with a long end table against the west wall. On top of which is a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a [silver jeweled necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Jeweled_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Jeweled Necklace"), a large coin purse and a bowl containing a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") and three bunches of juniper berries, while against the east wall is a tall wardrobe.

## Notes

- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the bottom left of the entrance door.
- During the Forsworn Conspiracy quest all or most of the occupants will be killed unless pickpocketing is used to acquire Thonar's Journal.
- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* mentions a character by the name of **Kolgrim** living here, although no such person exists, and is never mentioned in-game. No trace of this NPC can be found in the game data.

# Skyrim:The Ultimate Feast

## Overview

|  |  |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Spirits Away](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirits_Away "Skyrim:Spirits Away") | | → Next | [Beneath Bronze Waters](/wiki/Skyrim:Beneath_Bronze_Waters "Skyrim:Beneath Bronze Waters") | | |

The Ultimate Feast

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya") and read the [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Wanted:_A_Seafood_Feast "Skyrim:Wanted: A Seafood Feast").
2. Obtain [Steamed Mudcrab Legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamed_Mudcrab_Legs "Skyrim:Steamed Mudcrab Legs"), [Cooked Arctic Char](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Arctic_Char "Skyrim:Cooked Arctic Char"), and [Crab Stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Crab_Stew "Skyrim:Crab Stew").
3. Set the table in [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
4. Wait an hour and collect your tip.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This quest can be started after [Spirits Away](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirits_Away "Skyrim:Spirits Away") has been completed by talking to [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya"):

:   **Know of anyone in need of fishing work around Skyrim?**
:   *"You're headed to the capital. It's all in this note."*

She then hands you a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Wanted:_A_Seafood_Feast "Skyrim:Wanted: A Seafood Feast") that requests [Steamed Mudcrab Legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamed_Mudcrab_Legs "Skyrim:Steamed Mudcrab Legs"), [Cooked Arctic Char](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Arctic_Char "Skyrim:Cooked Arctic Char") and a bowl of [Crab Stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Crab_Stew "Skyrim:Crab Stew"). This will likely involve [cooking](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking").

You should have access to plenty of [Crab Meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Crab_Meat "Skyrim:Crab Meat") and [Mudcrab Legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab_Legs "Skyrim:Mudcrab Legs") after completing the [previous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirits_Away "Skyrim:Spirits Away"), and the other ingredients needed for the stew are not hard to acquire. [Butter](/wiki/Skyrim:Butter "Skyrim:Butter") can be a little trickier to find, although you can simply make your own at a churn if you've [constructed](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") a [kitchen](/wiki/Skyrim:Kitchen "Skyrim:Kitchen"). If you don't wish to go fishing for an [Arctic Char](/wiki/Skyrim:Arctic_Char "Skyrim:Arctic Char"), you can go diving at [Hela's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Hela%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Hela's Folly") instead and catch one with your hands.

Once you have obtained all three dishes, head to [The Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") and set the upstairs table for [Gisli](/wiki/Skyrim:Gisli "Skyrim:Gisli"). She will sit down to eat, which will take her an hour. Once she's finished, she'll leave a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Gisli%27s_Note "Skyrim:Gisli's Note") and a [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on the plate.

## Quest Stages

| The Ultimate Feast (ccBGSSSE001\_Misc\_Solitude) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |

The innkeeper does not stock everything she would like, so I'll need to collect all of the food in Gisli's bounty letter in order to set a table for her on the second floor of the Winking Skeever. *Objective 0:* Obtain a pair of steamed crab legs  *Objective 1:* Obtain a cooked arctic char  *Objective 2:* Obtain a bowl of crab stew  *Objective 50:* Set a table for Gisli at the Winking Skeever |
| 20 |  | I have set a table for Gisli at the Winking Skeever in Solitude. I should wait for her to take her seat and check in once she's finished dining. *Objective 29:* Wait for Gisli to take her seat  *Objective 30:* Wait an hour for Gisli to finish dining |
| 40 |  | Gisli should be finished dining by now. I should check the table for her payment. *Objective 40:* Check Gisli's table at the Winking Skeever |
| 200 | ☑ | I prepared a huge seafood feast for Gisli in Solitude. Judging by the letter of thanks and the coin purse left on her empty plate, she seemed satisfied with her meal. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 35, 250, 300.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Misc_Solitude stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Misc_Solitude`.

# Skyrim:The Underforge

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Guild Hall: The Underforge ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Underforge)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Underforge "Lore:Underforge")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| WhiterunUnderforge | |
| Region | |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | |
| Location | |
| Underneath the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge") behind [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") | |

The secret entrance to the Underforge

**The Underforge** is an ancient chamber hidden underneath the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge") used as a ritual chamber by the [Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle") of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").

Inside the Underforge

Like the Skyforge, its origins are unknown, and it was there before [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") was built and [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") was founded.

## Related Quests

- **[The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand")**: Join the ranks of [the Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle") and clear [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") of werewolf hunters.
- **[Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead")**: Cure [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")'s spirit and become Harbinger of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").
- **[Totems of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Totems_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Totems of Hircine")**: Journey to the given location to find a Totem of Hircine. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## The Underforge

The first time you visit the Underforge is during [The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand") quest, when you discover the secret of the senior members of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") and are invited to join the [Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle"). Its members describe it as an ancient place attuned to the moon and [Hircine](/wiki/Lore:Hircine "Lore:Hircine"). A font in the center of the room is a central part of the blood ritual and is filled with the blood of the initiate's "forebear". After drinking the blood, the initiate will begin the transformation into a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Lycanthropy "Skyrim:Lycanthropy"). There are three altars to Hircine around the room. These are initially empty, but after completing [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead"), [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") will give you quests to travel with her to seek these totems out, if you choose to remain a werewolf. The Underforge also contains a secret exit out to Skyrim that bypasses all the city guards and citizens, allowing for safe travel while transformed.

The exit brings you out a short distance north of [Battle-Born Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born_Farm "Skyrim:Battle-Born Farm"), with a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") to the left and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") above it. This exit cannot be used to re-enter [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") due to a ledge that you have to drop down to exit.

## The Totems of Hircine

The totems are described in detail in the tome *[The Totems of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Totems_of_Hircine "Skyrim:The Totems of Hircine")*. By praying to these totems you will be given a unique ability that can be activated while in [beast form](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Form "Skyrim:Beast Form").

- **Totem of Fear**: Causes [Fear](/wiki/Skyrim:Fear_(spell) "Skyrim:Fear (spell)")
- **Totem of Brotherhood**: Summons two [Pack Members](/wiki/Skyrim:Pack_Member "Skyrim:Pack Member")
- **Totem of The Hunt**: Grants [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(effect) "Skyrim:Detect Life (effect)")

## Notes

- Even at night, daylight can be seen shining through the holes in the walls.
- Sometimes when exiting the Underforge, you may find yourself underneath Whiterun entirely. If you're used to glitches, you might recognize the area you are in as the path to the hidden [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Merchant_Chests "Skyrim:Containers") under the Skyforge. If you have no interest in utilizing this exploit and to loot the merchant chest, you can simply fast travel.
  - Conditions for this bug occurred on Special Edition, Xbox One S, and only after becoming a werewolf for the second time.
- If you cure yourself of lycanthropy, you will no longer be able to enter the Underforge.

## Bugs

- The 3 Totems of Hircine may not give you their blessings if you pray at them. **?**
