# Skyrim:The Unquiet Dead

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Lay the spirits of Goldenhills Plantation to rest.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Reading [Restless Spirits bounty letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_-_Restless_Spirits "Skyrim:Bounty - Restless Spirits") or arriving at Goldenhills Plantation |
| Location(s): | [Goldenhills Plantation](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Goldenhills Plantation") |
| Reward: | [Key to Goldenhills Plantation](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Key to Goldenhills Plantation") |
| ID: | ccVSVSSE004\_MainQuest |
| Added by: | [Farming](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming "Skyrim:Farming") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** None | **Next →** [A Farmer's Life For Me](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Farmer%27s_Life_For_Me "Skyrim:A Farmer's Life For Me") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | None | | → Next | [A Farmer's Life For Me](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Farmer%27s_Life_For_Me "Skyrim:A Farmer's Life For Me") | | |

A haunted farm is up for grabs

## Quick Walkthrough

1. *(Optional)* Ask an innkeeper for work until you receive the [Restless Spirits bounty letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_-_Restless_Spirits "Skyrim:Bounty - Restless Spirits").
2. Travel to Goldenhills Plantation.
3. Investigate the plantation house.
4. Investigate the well.
5. Return to the plantation house.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Rin and the old well

You can start this quest by either asking an innkeeper for work until they give you [Bounty - Restless Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_-_Restless_Spirits "Skyrim:Bounty - Restless Spirits"), or you can simply head straight to Goldenhills Plantation.

As you arrive at [Goldenhills Plantation](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Goldenhills Plantation"), a ghost will attack you, after dealing with it you can collect the [torn page](/wiki/Skyrim:Torn_Page "Skyrim:Torn Page") next to the corpse of [Urval](/wiki/Skyrim:Urval "Skyrim:Urval"). Head inside and go to the top floor to find [Urval's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Urval%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Urval's Journal") which shows that Urval accused his wife of being a witch before attacking her, after which she appears to have poisoned him. The next step is to find her secret laboratory to uncover the truth, head down to the basement and look to the right as you enter, there is a button on the wall by the door, press it and the cupboard will move to reveal the secret lab.

Enter the laboratory and the ghost of [Jonquil](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonquil "Skyrim:Jonquil") will appear and attack you, after dealing with her, read the [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonquil%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Jonquil's Journal") on the apothecary table to discover the truth about what occurred at Goldenhills Plantation. After their son disappeared, Urval and Jonquil killed each other, Jonquil with extract of Deadly Nightshade, Urval with an axe each thinking that the other had murdered their son, Rin. To put their spirts to rest you need to discover what happened to Rin.

Head back upstairs to Rin's room, and look under his bed to find his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Rin%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Rin's Journal") which mentions that he was going to go to the old well to hunt a wolf. Leave the building and head southeast towards [Gjukar's Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjukar%27s_Monument "Skyrim:Gjukar's Monument"), as you are heading towards it, look to the left and you will see the old well surrounded by wolves. Once you have dispatched the wolves, take [Rin's toy sword](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Rin%27s_Toy_Sword&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Rin's Toy Sword (page does not exist)") from the child's skeleton.

Urval, Jonquil and Rin

Take the toy sword into Rin's room and place it under the Imperial banner, the ghosts of Urval, Jonquil and Rin will appear behind you. Speak to Rin:

:   **Your family can rest in peace now.**
:   *"Thanks a lot! Here. Take this. For all your hard work."*

The [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Key to Goldenhills Plantation") to the plantation will be placed in your inventory as a reward. The next quest, [A Farmer's Life For Me](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Farmer%27s_Life_For_Me "Skyrim:A Farmer's Life For Me") will then automatically start when you leave the house.

## Notes

- There's a [Nord War Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Unobtainable_Items#Nord_War_Horn "Skyrim:Unobtainable Items") in Rin's room, which is unobtainable otherwise, a unique Alembic in [Jonquil](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonquil "Skyrim:Jonquil")'s secret lab, a [Broken Iron War Axe Head](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots#Broken_Iron_War_Axe_Head "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots") and a [Broken Iron War Axe Handle](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots#Broken_Iron_War_Axe_Handle "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots") in the box on the second floor. They will disappear once the rooms are renovated.

## Bugs

- Quest won't start if the wolves at the old well are killed or have not loaded in before fighting the ghost outside of the house.
- The ghosts of Rin and his parents may not show up after placing the toy sword in Rin's room. This appears to happen after you've completed the quest and then reload a save from before completing it.
  - Restarting the game and then placing the toy sword should fix the issue. Restarting the game will also make the ghost of Rin's mother appear if she hasn't appeared before.
- Quest won't start if a follower or horse kills the ghost in the beginning.
- Quest won't start if Urval's corpse does not appear on site. This happens if the cell containing Urval’s corpse is loaded prematurely, causing his body to despawn after a time.
  - The sure way of triggering this quest is to confront Urval’s ghost the first time you’re in the vicinity of the plantation.
- The ghosts may not appear if you have a follower with you, especially if you have more than one.
  - You can avoid this by dismissing them before doing the quest or simply having your follower(s) wait outside the farmhouse.
- Quest won't update past "find out what happened to Rin" if you find his body and take his sword before this point.
  - To fix this place the sword in a weapon rack, then pick it up again.
- If the player leaves after killing the husband and returns at a later time, there is a chance that the ghosts in the house will not spawn, making the quest impossible to complete. **?**
  - This specifically occurs after reloading a save, regardless of location. It is best to complete the related quest in one sitting after killing the husband.

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 1, 10, 20, 50, 60, 70, 80, 90, 100, 300.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccVSVSSE004_MainQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccVSVSSE004_MainQuest`.

# Skyrim:The Warrens

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

The Warrens

**The Warrens** is a shelter for the sick and homeless in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

Hidden away a few feet from the Markarth Smelter, The Warrens is where the extreme lower-class citizens of Markarth reside: the miners and smelters, the sick and the lame. It consists of one area, *[The Warrens](#The_Warrens)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Cairine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cairine "Skyrim:Cairine")  [Cosnach](/wiki/Skyrim:Cosnach "Skyrim:Cosnach") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine")  [Dryston](/wiki/Skyrim:Dryston "Skyrim:Dryston")  [Eltrys](/wiki/Skyrim:Eltrys "Skyrim:Eltrys")  [Garvey](/wiki/Skyrim:Garvey "Skyrim:Garvey") [Trainer (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Expert)")[Sneak (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Sneak (Expert)")  [Hathrasil](/wiki/Skyrim:Hathrasil "Skyrim:Hathrasil")  [Omluag](/wiki/Skyrim:Omluag "Skyrim:Omluag") |

## Related Quests

- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").
- **[Fortunate Son](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortunate_Son "Skyrim:Fortunate Son")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"): Claim a fortune.[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")

## The Warrens

Inside the Warrens

The place is degrading and disgusting, evident by the sick [Cairine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cairine "Skyrim:Cairine") sitting on the floor all day long, warning you about the place. It contains six rooms for the inhabitants, all with owned hay piles and a sparse amount of belongings. Near the entrance stands [Garvey](/wiki/Skyrim:Garvey "Skyrim:Garvey"), a [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak"), 24 hours a day. There is absolutely nothing of value in the main hallway, with the exception of some [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") near the central fire.

The first door on the left leads to [Omluag](/wiki/Skyrim:Omluag "Skyrim:Omluag")'s room, with only two owned hay piles. The second door on the left leads to [Cosnach](/wiki/Skyrim:Cosnach "Skyrim:Cosnach")'s room, again only decorated with two hay piles. The third room on the left leads to [Eltrys](/wiki/Skyrim:Eltrys "Skyrim:Eltrys")' room, again with two hay piles, but also a bit of food, a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), two [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), two [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), and a harvested [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") mushroom. On the floor underneath the table sits the [key to Eltrys' room](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Eltrys%27s_Room "Skyrim:Key to Eltrys's Room").

The first door on the right leads to Garvey's private quarters and contains two hay piles and a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"). The next room is uninhabited, as falling boulders have covered it entirely. The next room belongs to [Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine") who owns absolutely nothing but the two hay piles. The last room on the right belongs to [Weylin](/wiki/Skyrim:Weylin "Skyrim:Weylin") and is the place you will have to search during the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy"). It contains a hay pile, a table with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a rock warbler egg, and a slice of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). On a small ledge near the chair sits the [key to Weylin's room](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Weylin%27s_Room "Skyrim:Key to Weylin's Room"). Lastly, a chest in the corner contains some gold and random loot and the quest-related [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Weylin%27s_Note "Skyrim:Weylin's Note") needed to investigate the Forsworn Conspiracy. With [Bittercup](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, a vault will also be present in the Warrens, which you'll need to visit to finish "Fortunate Son".

## Notes

- There is an "Empty" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the top left of the entrance door, marking the lack of valuable items inside.
- If you infect Cairine with vampirism during the [New Allegiances](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Allegiances "Skyrim:New Allegiances")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") quest, a coffin will appear in the room shared by Garvey and Cairine and can be used to sleep and get the vampire rested bonus. Cairine does not seem to use it however, nor does Garvey seem too fazed by it, although he never seems to sleep either.
- Despite what both Cairine and Garvey say, no one that lives here is actually sick with any diseases you can catch. In *Skyrim*, only wild creatures (and vampires) can distribute diseases.
- The Warrens appear in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") as the [Underhall](/wiki/Online:Underhall "Online:Underhall").

# Skyrim:The Way of the Voice

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |

Master Borri teaching "Wuld"

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead").
2. Climb the 7,000 Steps.
3. Speak to the Greybeards at [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar").

### Ivarstead

After you're finished in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), you'll want to head to [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), as it is located at the foot of the 7,000 Steps leading up to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar"). Once you get there and get close to the bridge, you'll hear a conversation. Talk to one of the men, [Klimmek](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek "Skyrim:Klimmek"), and learn about what dangers are lurking ahead. You can take an [optional quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Climb_the_Steps "Skyrim:Climb the Steps") from him to deliver supplies to the Greybeards. You may also ask people there to tell you some information about High Hrothgar:

| Name | Response |
| --- | --- |
| **[Wilhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Wilhelm "Skyrim:Wilhelm")** | *"The Greybeards are a solitary lot. I don't think they've ever ventured outside their monastery. We get the occasional pilgrim passing through here on their way to the summit, but almost all of them have returned disappointed."* |
| **[Klimmek](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek "Skyrim:Klimmek")** | *"I've been to the monastery many times, but I've never even laid eyes on one of the Greybeards. Not that I'd care to. Being masters of the Thu'um, they could kill you by uttering a single word. Well, not that they would. They seem peaceful, but I wouldn't want to provoke them. "* |
| **[Bassianus Axius](/wiki/Skyrim:Bassianus_Axius "Skyrim:Bassianus Axius")** | *"Klimmek brings food supplies up to them once every few weeks when the weather permits it. Other than that, they seem like a quiet lot. Don't really know too much about them."* |
| **[Boti](/wiki/Skyrim:Boti "Skyrim:Boti")** | *"It's frightening living below their monastery. Sometimes I swear I can hear strange noises rolling down from up there. It sounds like thunder, but there's never any rain. What do you make of that?"* |
| **[Temba Wide-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Temba_Wide-Arm "Skyrim:Temba Wide-Arm")** | *"The Greybeards stay away from me, and I stay away from them. Suits me just fine."* |
| **[Gwilin](/wiki/Skyrim:Gwilin "Skyrim:Gwilin")** | *"Always thought it was odd that there's a layer of thick clouds covering the peak of the mountain above the monastery. Not sure what's up there, but I bet the Greybeards know."* |
| **[Jofthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Jofthor "Skyrim:Jofthor")** | *"They call the path to the monastery the 7,000 Steps. Can you imagine? I'm not certain if I could even make it to the top without collapsing from exhaustion."* |
| **[Fastred](/wiki/Skyrim:Fastred "Skyrim:Fastred")** | *"The Greybeards are a strange bunch. I heard they live their entire life without uttering a single word; can you even imagine?"* |
| **[Lynly Star-Sung](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynly_Star-Sung "Skyrim:Lynly Star-Sung")** | *"I've always fancied a journey up the 7,000 Steps to the monastery. Anything to break the boredom of living in this town. I envy you."* |

### The 7,000 Steps

When you start on the trail up, you'll run across various leveled wildlife and monsters, and a couple of pilgrims, [Barknar](/wiki/Skyrim:Barknar "Skyrim:Barknar") and [Karita](/wiki/Skyrim:Karita_(warrior) "Skyrim:Karita (warrior)"). You will also find various etched stone tablets ("emblems") giving you information on the history of the [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") and the [Way of the Voice](/wiki/Lore:Way_of_the_Voice "Lore:Way of the Voice").

There is an iron ore vein hidden near the third emblem shrine. Once the third shrine is in view climb the small hill to your right. It is at the top of the hill hidden from view of the main walking path.

Shortly after the fourth emblem where you meet Karita, at a point where the steps are sandwiched between two cliffs, there is a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") that will jump from the top of one cliff if it sees you (though sometimes it may be found further up the path). For low-level characters, this can be a difficult fight. It can be avoided altogether by sneaking past it at night or scaling the cliffs nearby.

#### Combat Strategies

1. Frost trolls, like any other type of troll, have a weakness to fire. Thus, handy combat strategies include using weapons which have a fire enchantment, using fire-based destruction spells, and [summoning a flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Flame Atronach"). The Shout [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath") could also be used, as a word for it can be gained early on in the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") questline. If you are a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf"), your [Ancestors Wrath](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestor%27s_Wrath "Skyrim:Ancestor's Wrath") power will also work.
2. Trolls can deal a substantial amount of damage, but most of it can be avoided by tactically falling back when one sees the troll raising his arms or preparing a power attack. If you need to heal, you can sprint away; the troll will not generally outrun you. Similarly, using a shield to block the Troll's attacks can also be effective, but does depend highly on timing.
3. It is possible to scale the rocks just before the troll, allowing you to use ranged attacks to safely eliminate it. However, the troll may regenerate its health faster than you can damage it. Using a bow with a fire enchantment or ranged destruction spells such as [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt") would give an advantage.
4. If you are careful, it can be killed by long distance arrows from the entrance to the ravine it lives in. Go into stealth mode, stand at the entrance to the ravine, all to the right, and shoot at the troll when you can just see it on top of the cliff. If done properly, the troll may shift left or right a little, but will not come after you; the x2 sneak attack bonus (x3 with the perk) should allow you to kill it quickly. However, if it falls off the cliff, this will not work anymore.
5. You can lure the troll up to High Hrothgar, and the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout will briefly help you move faster. If the troll follows you into the monastery, the Greybeards will defeat it very quickly.
6. If you retreat down the stairs, [Karita](/wiki/Skyrim:Karita_(warrior) "Skyrim:Karita (warrior)"), who is meditating at the tablet, will help defeat the troll.

#### Avoiding the Fight

1. It is easily possible to simply run past the Troll, as it moves rather slowly.
2. [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") can use their racial power [Battle Cry](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_Cry "Skyrim:Battle Cry") to make the troll flee for 30 seconds, giving you enough time to run to High Hrothgar. Similarly, a [Bosmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") can use [Command Animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Command_Animal "Skyrim:Command Animal") to calm the troll. You can also use [Animal Allegiance](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Allegiance "Skyrim:Animal Allegiance") to calm the troll.
3. You can use [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") at the troll, then sprint away before the stun effect wears off.
4. You can scale the rocks to the left of the ravine, and you'll never be detected at all.

### The Greybeards

High Hrothgar

After finally arriving at High Hrothgar, you'll be greeted by [Master Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir"), who speaks to you on behalf of the other [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") (whose voices are too powerful for conversation). After proving you are the Dragonborn by using the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout, they welcome you to their monastery and instruct you on how to use the dragon shouts, or Thu'um.

To further your training in the ways of the Thu'um, you will be taught the second word to the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout, *Ro*, and asked to practice it three times on [ethereal targets](/wiki/Skyrim:Phantom_Form "Skyrim:Phantom Form") that the Greybeards summon. Arngeir comments on how quickly you learn, then takes you outside for the next lesson. They teach you another word for [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"). You'll be asked to practice it by using the shout to get through the gate [Master Borri](/wiki/Skyrim:Borri "Skyrim:Borri") opens before it closes. When you're finished, Arngeir will send you on the last test: retrieving [the Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller"). Upon completion of this quest, you will gain access to the [main quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)") of the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") expansion.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **The Way of the Voice** (20 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- During the quest, [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") and [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") have additional dialogs talking about Greybeards.
- If you activate and read all ten plaques along the 7,000 Steps, you'll receive the blessing [Voice of the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Voice_of_the_Sky "Skyrim:Voice of the Sky") that causes wildlife to neither flee nor attack you for 24 hours.
- There appear to be only around 700 steps, but many may have been worn down or covered in snow over time.
- If you consider steps as paces rather than stairs, there are around 2000 steps (when using the walking animation)
- With a [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") and a little cunning, you can skip both the long trip to Ivarstead and climbing the 7,000 Steps altogether. Starting at the [Whiterun Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Stormcloak Camp"), you can ride almost straight up the mountain, bypassing the dangerous creatures and the tedious long climb with only moderate difficulty.
- If you bypass Ivarstead and the two pilgrims on the way up in this way, Karita will never be encountered, since she is set to disappear from the game once the player reaches High Hrothgar. Barknar will still be there at his position, on the way down, and so will Klimmek in Ivarstead, with his quest to deliver the goods. Unfortunately, the Frost Troll will also be there - although of course, fast-travelling directly from High Hrothgar avoids it (and all the above).
- The shout the Greybeards use to create the attack targets for learning Ro is [Fiik Lo Sah](/wiki/Skyrim:Phantom_Form "Skyrim:Phantom Form"), Mirror Deceive Phantom. It is not attainable by the player except through console codes.
- When you are asked to run through the gate before it closes using your new Whirlwind Sprint shout, you can make it through the gate in time using a regular sprint.
- Arngeir's dialogue about Whirlwind Sprint is slightly different if you already know a word of the shout. If you have learned part of the shout through word walls, you will receive the second or third part of the shout instead.

## Bugs

- If you enter High Hrothgar from the back door (where you perform the shout "whirlwind sprint"), the Greybeards may not congregate in the hall and the quest will not progress (stuck on "speak to Arngeir"). Exit from the front door and re-enter before speaking to [Master Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir") to progress.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- The Greybeards may attack you after you use an Unrelenting Force on them.
- If you leave High Hrothgar after being presented the word *Ro*, but before learning (absorbing) the word on the floor, you may not be able to learn the word when you return. This can also happen in very rare cases even if you do not leave (more likely to happen later in the game if you have put off doing the main quest). This can break the main quest. There is no workaround for this other than reloading a previous save from before the word is presented to you.
- If you interrupt Einarth while he's casting *Ro* on the floor by talking to him or shouting at him, it may not appear. **?**
  - Save and re-load the game, and he should resume the casting.
- When asked to demonstrate the Voice, the spectres may not appear.
  - Open your inventory and close it again and the spectre should appear.
- When asked to demonstrate the Voice, spectre appear endlessly without progessing to the next quest stage. Use console command *setstage 90*.
- In demonstrating Whirlwind Sprint, [Master Wulfgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulfgar "Skyrim:Wulfgar") may inadvertently send himself flying off the mountain. **?**
- If you interrupt Borri in the courtyard, just before, or as you are told to approach him so that he can impart his understand of the whirlwind sprit shout. The quest can bug, and no matter how long you wait, or prompt him - He will just make the motion/animation movement, but he will not impart the 'understanding.' Leaving you stuck (This bug has only been reported happening when you have Serana with you. Which might be relevant as it seems to prompt her audio response as if you talked to her). **?**
  - The easiest way to resolve this is simply to load the autosave from when you entered the courtyard.

I spoke to Arngeir, one of the Greybeards, who believes that I am "Dragonborn", which means I am especially gifted in the use of the Voice. They have offered to help me learn to use my new abilities. *Objective 20:* Demonstrate your "Unrelenting Force" Shout |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQ105 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQ105`.

# Skyrim:The Whispering Door

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Daedric.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Daedric.png) | **Investigate [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir")'s story of a Whispering Lady behind a locked door.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda"), [Jarl Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") |
| Reward: | [Ebony Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Blade "Skyrim:Ebony Blade") |
| ID: | DA08RumorPointer DA08 |
| Required Items: | [Whispering Door Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispering_Door_Key "Skyrim:Whispering Door Key") |
| Required Level: | 20 |
| Difficulty: | Medium |
| --- | |
| |  | | --- | | **Prerequisites:** [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") | | |

*You know her, don't you?*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to the innkeeper of [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") in Whiterun.
2. Ask Jarl [Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") about his children.
3. Talk to [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir").
4. Investigate the old wooden door in the basement.
5. Talk to Nelkir again.
6. Acquire the key from Balgruuf the Greater or [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire").
7. Open the door.
8. Retrieve the [Ebony Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Blade "Skyrim:Ebony Blade").

### A Disturbed Youth

Speaking with the publican at [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") about rumors can have them reveal to you that there is trouble in the Jarl's family.

:   *Been hearing some strange tales of the Jarl's children. Say the one's turning wicked, and the others have an ill-favored look to them. Best to keep clear."*

You can ask the Jarl himself, [Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater"), about it. Initially, he is situated within Dragonsreach, but if the player sided with the Stormcloaks in the Civil War, he will be in the Blue Palace basement. He will eventually express concerns that his youngest son, [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir"), has become exceptionally brooding: *"Yes, my youngest son. He's a dark child. I don't know what to do with him. He was always a quiet lad, but lately... something has changed. He's become brooding. Violent. He won't say a word to me, but I don't know how I upset him. If you could speak to him. Draw out the truth. I would be immensely grateful."*

Nelkir (who is always in Dragonsreach, regardless of where his father is), will be surprisingly forthcoming if you speak to him.

:   **Your father said to speak to you.**
:   *"So the disgusting pig sent you to bother me? One day, I'll tear his face apart so he can leave me alone. My father doesn't know anything about me. But I know about him. And about the war. More than he might think."*
:   **What sorts of things?**
:   *"I know that he still worships Talos. That he hates the Thalmor almost as much as the Stormcloaks do. That he worries about being chased from Whiterun. That he... that I'm... that I don't have the same mother as my brother and sister."*
:   **How do you know these things?**
:   *"This castle is old. Lots of places nobody's been in a long while. Places where you can overhear things. See things. And the Whispering Lady."*
:   **Who's the Whispering Lady?**
:   *"She won't tell me her name. I've gotten good at listening to keyholes. At the door in the basement, I hear her talking to me. I thought I was caught, but she started telling me even more secrets. But I can't open the door."*
:   **Where is this door?**
:   *"In the basement. Trust me, you'll see it. I bet she'll talk to you, too."*

### The Whispering Lady

The Ebony Blade

The door is actually well hidden in plain sight off the main hall of Dragonsreach. In order to find it, go into the kitchen. Proceed down the stairs and open the closet door in the small servant's room. At the back of the closet is a locked door which seems to be covered in blood. Activate the door, and the disembodied voice of the [Whispering Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispering_Lady "Skyrim:Whispering Lady") will begin talking to you.

:   **(Listen at the door)**
:   *"At last. I've been waiting for someone more fit to carry out my will. The child is spirited, but lacks... agency.*
:   **Is there someone behind the door?**
:   *"Regrettably, I cannot reach your plane so directly. But I forgive you for not knowing who I am. Few hear my whispers anymore. I am Mephala, the Lady of Whispers. I tug at the web of connections between mortals. Love, hatred, loyalty, betrayal. The boy was good at sussing out secrets. You, I expect to take a more active role."*
:   **What could the boy not do?**
:   *"The boy is good at sussing out secrets, but the corruptibility of children is ultimately too limited for my purposes. You, though, I expect will prove far more malleable."*

If you had asked her the latter question, there will be another stage of dialogue before the dialogue paths merge together again.

:   **Who are you to expect anything?**
:   *"I forgive your not knowing my name. Few can hear my whispers anymore. I am Mephala, the Lady of Whispers. I tug at the web of connections between mortals. Love, hatred, loyalty, betrayal."*
:   **I'm not so easily molded.**
:   *"You may think so. But in the end, you mortals will always flit like fire with the winds of your desires and conveniences. And those winds issue from my whispers."*

At this point you will either confirm you are willing to help, or refuse to.

:   **What do you want me to do?**
:   *"First, you must open this door. A piece of my power has been locked away behind it, and even my eyes cannot see past the seals. I'd much rather it be in the hands of an ambitious and talented person such as yourself."*
:   **I don't want to help you.**
:   *"Suit yourself. But those who listen at doors always wonder what is beyond them. Eventually your curiosity will drive you back to me."*

Regardless of your previous choice, you will now only have one option if you continue to speak to the door.

:   **How do I open the door?**
:   *"The whole of Whiterun is ripe*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *with paranoia and tensions. The Jarl's court is right to fear the power I hold behind this door. The Jarl trusts few, and they will be his undoing. The dark child knows of what I speak. Let him guide your path."*

Return to Nelkir to learn how you can go about getting the key to the door.

:   **Do you know how to open the Whispering Door?**
:   *"I told you, I know everything about this castle. For some reason that door is special. Only two people can open it, Balgruuf and Farengar, the court wizard. How you get it from them is up to you. Nobody would notice if Farengar went missing, I promise you."*

### Opening the Door

Nelkir will tell you that only the Jarl and the court mage, [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire"), possess a key to the Whispering Door, and suggests that Farengar will not be missed should he disappear. You can either track down the Jarl, who is either in his quarters or in the Blue Palace, or his wizard. Farengar will always be situated in Dragonsreach, even if the Jarl is now a prisoner of the Civil War. As for the key itself, you can pickpocket the [Whispering Door key](/wiki/Skyrim:Whispering_Door_Key "Skyrim:Whispering Door Key") off either Farengar or Balgruuf, or you can follow Nelkir's advice to kill Farengar and take it from his corpse. When you have the key, head down to the basement and open the door, which reveals a small room with a sword and a book resting on a table. The book, *[Admonition Against Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Admonition_Against_Ebony "Skyrim:Admonition Against Ebony")*, warns you against taking the sword lying next to it; however, to complete the quest, simply ignore the warning and pick up the sword. Mephala will speak to you again.

:   *"Excellent work. Now, I trust you're sharp enough to see that the sword doesn't match the description of the Ebony Blade you may know. It has languished too long outside the winds of alliance and betrayal. To return to its past glory, it must first drink the blood of deceit. To return to its past glory, it must reacquaint itself with the hatred of this world. Your world is admirably seeped in lies and inclinations. My blade is a darling leech that feeds on deceptions, and nourishes its master. Seek out those closest to you. The final pluck of their misguided heartstrings will accompany my blade in the song of your grandeur."*

If you choose to restore the blade, it requires staining with the blood of treachery. However, the blade's restoration is not necessary to complete the quest, simply its retrieval. Also, while you do not receive any further information on Nelkir's condition, if there are any subsequent interactions there seems to be an improvement in disposition. If you do choose to use the blade as Mephala has instructed, she will speak to you again each time you kill a friend.

:   *"Excellent work, child."*
:   *"I can feel their heartbreak swelling in my blade."*
:   *"Their tears shine the ebony to a sharpest gleam."*
:   *"Ah, the blood of deceit is a nourishing flow."*

After you perform the final needed kill, Mephala will speak to you a final time to congratulate you.

:   *"At last, my blade is returned to its full glory. Now go forth, child. Continue your tiny subversions against the orders of trust and intimacy."*

## Notes

- Several leftover elements in the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit") show that a portion of the quest was omitted from the final game. Originally, Jarl Balgruuf's children were all supposed to fall under Mephala's influence one by one, kill [Dagny's pet horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Karinda "Skyrim:Karinda"), and then finally culminating in them killing Balgruuf in an act of patricide. His brother [Hrongar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrongar "Skyrim:Hrongar") would have replaced him as jarl upon death, given that he has unused dialogue mirroring Balgruuf's for several quests, and some citizens of Whiterun, like [Ulfberth War-Bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfberth_War-Bear "Skyrim:Ulfberth War-Bear") have unused dialogue referring to Hrongar as jarl.
  -  While the original English dialogue for the unused portions of the quest was seemingly overwritten, the Polish localization still has all unused dialogue for Proventus, Nelkir, Frothar, and Dagny intact, shedding light on how their corruption and the buildup to Balgruuf's death would've transpired.
- The quest is still available if you have completed [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). Jarl Balgruuf will move from Dragonsreach to the basement of the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), but his dialogue will not change and the quest can still be completed normally.
- Despite Farengar allegedly being aware of the blade, you can still sell it to him.
- Should Farengar have died before the quest starts, then you can only get the key from Balgruuf.
- If you attempt to enter the room behind the Old Wooden Door using the "Platter Exploit" before you have completed the necessary steps in the quest, you will find a floating end table blocking your entry into the room; this is the source of Mephala's voice before unlocking the door. The sword, however, can still be seen on top of the table where it usually sits.

## Bugs

- Hulda is necessary for this rumor to unlock. Ysolda can take over as publican of The Bannered Mare if Hulda dies, but she will not give the rumor.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, addresses this issue. [Mikael](/wiki/Skyrim:Mikael "Skyrim:Mikael") will replace Hulda instead of Ysolda, as he has dialogue to give the quest.
  - Speaking to the jarl and asking about his kids will not activate this quest.
  - You must have completed the [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") quest to receive the rumor from Hulda.
- Hulda may not show any new rumors available after you are level 20. Try talking to her anyway; she may give you an old rumor, then follow up with this one. If this does not work, the console command `setstage DA08 10` will initiate the quest and give you a quest marker to speak to Nelkir.
- There may not be a dialogue option with the jarl after receiving the quest.
- If [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda") and [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") both die, you cannot get this quest.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.5, addresses this issue. Ysolda is now marked as [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs").

## Quest Stages

| 25 |  | Mephala, the Lady of Whispers, has tasked me with releasing the Ebony Blade from its prison. *Objective 25:* Speak to Nelkir |

| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Retrieve the Ebony Blade |

| ☑ | I have received Mephala's Ebony Blade, but it lacks its legendary powers. To restore it, I must achieve great infamy and hatred in this land. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table:

  - DA08: 0, 1, 51.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DA08RumorPointer
  DA08 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DA08RumorPointer
  DA08`.

# Skyrim:The White Hall

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

| *[Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Weapon_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments")*  *[The Art of War Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Art_of_War_Magic "Skyrim:The Art of War Magic")* | |

| # of [Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") | 1 |

The White Hall

**The White Hall** is a large two-story structure that sits on a hillside overlooking most of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). It is found next door to [Dawnstar Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Barracks "Skyrim:Dawnstar Barracks").

The hall is home to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") as well as their court and servant. It contains only one area: *[The White Hall](#The_White_Hall)*.

## Residents

| [Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald") | [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") | [Brina Merilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis") |

| [Jod](/wiki/Skyrim:Jod "Skyrim:Jod") | [Housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") | [Horik Halfhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Horik_Halfhand "Skyrim:Horik Halfhand") |
| [Frorkmar Banner-Torn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frorkmar_Banner-Torn "Skyrim:Frorkmar Banner-Torn") | Military Advisor | [Legate Constantius Tituleius](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Constantius_Tituleius "Skyrim:Legate Constantius Tituleius") |

## Related Quests

- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Giant_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Giant (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") by killing a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Thane of the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale")**: Gain the title of [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Wave Breaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Wave_Breaker "Skyrim:Wave Breaker")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") is threatened by a [giant crab](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Crab_Guardian_Spirit "Skyrim:Emperor Crab Guardian Spirit")!

### Exterior

There are several [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes on either side of the front of the building. There is a short flight of steps leading up to the main door. When you first arrive in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") you can witness an interesting exchange between [Skald](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald") and [Brina Merilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis") with [Horik Halfhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Horik_Halfhand "Skyrim:Horik Halfhand") in attendance on the steps in front of the building.

### The White Hall

Jarl's court

Upon entering you are at the end of the main room where the Jarl holds court. The Jarl sits on their throne during the day with their [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") beside them. On either side of the room there are small round wooden tables holding bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). There are two round firepits down the center of the room with the throne at the end on a slightly raised platform. There are two flights of stairs—one against the west wall and the other against the east, both of which lead to balconies and small bedrooms on the top floor. Under the stairs there is a doorway to the east and a door to the west. The west opens into the Jarl's bedroom and the east leads to the room used by the military advisor and where the court wizard [Madena](/wiki/Skyrim:Madena "Skyrim:Madena") sells her wares. There are Dawnstar banners hanging from the walls above the throne.

Madena's stock

The doorway to the east leads to a room with six weapon racks holding a selection of [iron weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") along the west wall with two barrels in front. There are two [potions of plentiful stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina") and three [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on top of the barrels. On the ground by the northern barrel is a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Weapon_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments")*. Against the north wall are a couple of straw bales with a practice dummy in front of them. To the right of the bales is a long wooden table with three bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") marking the progress, if any, of the civil war. The military advisor will spend most of their time studying this. In the corner to the right are a couple of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels.

Along the east wall there is a large pile of firewood beside an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Above the chest, on top of a wall shelf, are several potions that can be bought from Madena (see [notes](#Notes)). There are more food barrels in the southeastern corner. On your right as soon as you enter the room, against the south wall, is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), with a wall shelf above it holding more potions sold by Madena. To the left of the enchanter is an L-shaped counter, with a bottle of alto wine, a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and some ingredients sold by Madena on top of it (see [notes](#Notes)). Under the counter is a medium coin purse. Against the south wall behind the counter are two sets of shelves full of items sold by Madena (see [notes](#Notes)).

The Jarl's bedroom consists of a king-sized bed in the middle of the room on a raised platform with four tall and one small wardrobe all containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") along the west wall. There are several food barrels and sacks around the room. Against the south wall is a large round wooden table and two chairs. On the table is a bottle of alto wine and a bottle of wine. Against the north wall is a long unlocked chest containing minor loot and to the right of this is a second round table and two chairs. On this table is a bottle of alto wine, two bottles of wine, a large coin purse and seven loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). There is also a long wooden bench along the east wall.

The balcony to the east has a small round wooden table holding three bottles of Nord mead and a chair beside it. Several barrels and a larger round wooden table and chair. On this table is a bottle of Nord mead, a bottle of alto wine and a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[The Art of War Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Art_of_War_Magic "Skyrim:The Art of War Magic")*. There is also a door to a bedroom, which continues farther east.

The bedroom has an owned single bed against the east wall, in the northeastern corner, with a small wardrobe to the left of it. On the wardrobe there is a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust") and a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"). Farther along the east wall is a long unlocked chest containing minor loot. In the southeastern corner is a food barrel with a large coin purse and five loose coins on top. Next to it, against the south wall, is a set of shelves holding a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a copy of *[The Talos Mistake](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Talos_Mistake "Skyrim:The Talos Mistake")*, a copy of *[Treatise on Ayleidic Cities](/wiki/Skyrim:Treatise_on_Ayleidic_Cities "Skyrim:Treatise on Ayleidic Cities")*, three [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), a medium coin purse, a bottle of Nord mead, two bottles of alto wine and four bottles of wine. Next to the shelves is a chair.

The balcony to the west has two bales of straw stacked in the northwestern corner and a round wooden table in front of them with two chairs. On the table are two bottles of Nord mead and a bottle of alto wine. There are several barrels on the balcony, one of which has a bottle of alto wine on top.

The bedroom has an owned single bed against the west wall in the northwestern corner. Opposite it, against the east wall, is a long unlocked chest. In the middle of the south wall is a set of shelves holding three [green](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), two [flutes](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), three lockicks, an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel") and a goat cheese wheel and a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") leaning against the front of it. On either side are food sacks, with a chair to the right and two [drums](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") next to the chair. To the left of the door as you enter there is a wall shelves holding a potion of minor healing, a potion of minor magicka, two red and three green apples.

### Displayed Merchandise Sold by Madena

- The following items are sitting out in the room on the counter or shelves. They can be purchased if you have the relevant [skill perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Perks "Skyrim:Skill Perks") (see [notes](#Notes)) or taken for free if your [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") towards Madena is high enough. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

**Potions**: 1 [draught of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Draught of Enhanced Stamina"), 1 [draught of illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Illusion "Skyrim:Draught of Illusion"), 4 [potions of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"), 1 [potion of illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Illusion "Skyrim:Potion of Illusion"), 1 [potion of lasting potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Potion of Lasting Potency"), 2 [potion of lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lockpicking "Skyrim:Potion of Lockpicking"), 4 [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), 2 [potions of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), 1 [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"). |

## Notes

- All of the [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") and [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") on the shelves and counter only are sold by Madena, once you have the [Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Merchant "Skyrim:Speech") [skill perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Perks "Skyrim:Skill Perks"). They have all been listed under [Displayed Merchandise Sold by Madena](#Displayed_Merchandise_Sold_by_Madena)

## Bugs

- Brina Merilis, Horik Halfhand, and Skald the Elder may be stuck outside the longhouse if Dawnstar is handed over to the Imperials before the player has ever been there.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

The entrance to the White Phial

**The White Phial** is the alchemical shop located on the north side of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")'s market district.

The owner is [Nurelion](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion"), who named the shop after the legendary artifact he's spent many years searching for. When Nurelion is not available, the shop duties are handled by his assistant, [Quintus Navale](/wiki/Skyrim:Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Quintus Navale").

## Residents

| Name |
| --- |
| [Nurelion](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") [Alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Alchemist")  [Quintus Navale](/wiki/Skyrim:Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Quintus Navale") [Alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Alchemist") |

## Related Quests

- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)")**: Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## The White Phial

The interior

When entering the shop the counter is in front of you down the length of the room with an end piece to the right and stairs up to the residence against the east wall. There is a square table and two chairs to the left, against the south wall, while in the southeastern corner is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). There are [displayed merchandise](#Displayed_Merchandise) on the counter, under the counter, on the square table to the left, on the two sets of shelves and another square table behind the counter, against the north wall. There are additionally several sacks and barrels containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") throughout the shop and residence.

In addition to these items there is a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a [mammoth cheese bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl") on the counter, a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Black Arts On Trial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Arts_On_Trial "Skyrim:The Black Arts On Trial")*, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") under the counter, three [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") on the table against the north wall, with an empty [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem") on a stand beside it and a [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") on one of the shelves. To the west is a doorway into a storeroom, which is also used by [Quintus Navale](/wiki/Skyrim:Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Quintus Navale") as a bedroom. It is filled with crates, sacks, barrels, a cart filled with floor rugs and in the middle of the room a single bed with an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") by the foot of it and a basket containing a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") and two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") by the head.

At the top of the stairs is a dining and kitchen area with a long wooden table and benches in the center of the room, with a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") on the table and an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie") under it. The floorboards on this level have several holes in them. In the southeastern corner is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand with two racks hanging from a beam to the left, holding two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). In an alcove on the south wall is a set of shelves holding two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") among loads of clutter, with a chair to the right of it. Further along the south wall is an end table with a master-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") on top and a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") to the right. There is a doorway on the west wall, with another set of shelves to the left of it holding a gourd and more clutter.

Nurelion's bedroom

The doorway leads into [Nurelion](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion")'s bedroom, which contains an owned double bed coming out from the west wall, with an end table to the left, against the south wall with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top and a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") beside it. While to the right of the bed, against the north wall is a dresser with the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger"), a bottle of Nord mead and a copy of *[Harvesting Frostbite Spider Venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Harvesting_Frostbite_Spider_Venom "Skyrim:Harvesting Frostbite Spider Venom")* all on top. To the right of the dresser, in the middle of the north wall, is an unlit fireplace with a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") to the left, a cauldron to the right and a chair in front of it. Finally in the southeastern corner is a round wooden table and chair.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or else can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

- Ingredients: 1 [Bleeding Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), 2 [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), 1 [Chaurus Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), 3 [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), 2 [Dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), 1 [Fire Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), 1 [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), 1 [Frost Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), 1 [Garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), 1 [Giant Lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen"), 2 [Grass Pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod"), 2 [Hagraven Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), 1 [Hagraven Feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), 2 [Hanging Moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss"), 1 [Imp Stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), 2 [Jazbay Grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), 2 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), 2 [Nordic Barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"), 1 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), 1 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), 1 [Rock Warbler Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), 3 [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), 3 [Scaly Pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), 1 [Skeever Tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), 3 [Slaughterfish Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), 1 [Slaughterfish Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), 1 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), 2 [Spider Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"), 1 [Swamp Fungal Pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod"), 1 [Taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), 1 [Thistle Branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), 1 [Troll Fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), 1 [Vampire Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), 1 [White Cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap")
- Ingredient (req. [Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_(perk) "Skyrim:Merchant (perk)") perk): 1 [Orange Dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing")
- Poison (req. [Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_(perk) "Skyrim:Merchant (perk)") perk): 1 [Frostbite Venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom")
- Potions: 1 [Draught of Extra Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Draught of Extra Magicka"), 1 [Draught of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Health "Skyrim:Draught of Health"), 2 [Draught of Lasting Potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Draught of Lasting Potency"), 1 [Draught of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), 1 [Potion of Enhanced Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"), 1 [Potion of Extra Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"), 1 [Potion of Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), 1 [Potion of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), 1 [Potion of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), 3 [Potion of Minor Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), 1 [Potion of Minor Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), 1 [Potion of Pickpocketing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Pickpocketing "Skyrim:Potion of Pickpocketing"), 1 [Potion of Plentiful Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Magicka"), 2 [Potion of Resist Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Cold "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Cold"), 1 [Potion of Resist Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), 2 [Potion of Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), 1 [Solution of Vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Solution of Vigor")

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the White Phial's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") every two days.

## Notes

- Nurelion can still be heard yelling at you for loitering in his store even when no interaction with him is possible.
- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the right of the store's sign.

## Bugs

- The shop has no fire burning in Nurelion's fireplace, so he sits there staring at nothing.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
