# Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Nurelion](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") in [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(place) "Skyrim:The White Phial (place)") |
| Location(s): | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), [Forsaken Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Cave "Skyrim:Forsaken Cave") |
| Reward: | 5 gold, followed by 500 gold Word for the [Marked for Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Marked_for_Death "Skyrim:Marked for Death") shout |
| ID: | MS12 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial") (finish [The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World") first) | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial") (finish [The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World") first) | | |

The White Phial on a pedestal in a secret room

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Nurelion](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") in his [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") store.
2. Retrieve the White Phial from [Forsaken Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Cave "Skyrim:Forsaken Cave").
3. Return the Phial to Nurelion.
4. Talk to his assistant, [Quintus Navale](/wiki/Skyrim:Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Quintus Navale"), for your final reward.

### His Last Hope

The only [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") shop in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is called [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(place) "Skyrim:The White Phial (place)") and is located in the market district, right next to [Aval Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron")'s stall. When you enter you will witness a very sick and elderly proprietor, [Nurelion](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion"), trying to convince his assistant that he is able to make some kind of journey. The assistant, [Quintus Navale](/wiki/Skyrim:Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Quintus Navale"), is quite skeptical and with good reasons, as his master coughs constantly in between words:

*"Master, you're far too old for this sort of journey."*

**Nurelion**: *"I'll be fine."*
**Quintus**: *"Master, you're far too old for this sort of journey. We don't know what's inside..."*
**Nurelion**: *"I'll... I can... just..."*
**Quintus**: *"You see, you're not well! Have a seat and I'll fetch you some tonic."*
**Nurelion**: *"Bah. If there was a tonic that could help me, I would have found it by now..."*

After the discussion, Nurelion will take his place behind the counter and Quintus will walk away. Ask Nurelion what the argument was about and he will explain: *"Just a man's life work, is all. I've finally derived the location of the White Phial, but this doting busybody won't let me get it."* He is obviously referring to Quintus, but offer to help him find whatever he is looking for and he will provide some background information: *"It's buried with its maker, [Curalmil](/wiki/Skyrim:Curalmil "Skyrim:Curalmil"), in a long forsaken cave to the west of here. Curalmil was a crafty one, even in death. You would need the skills of a master alchemist to reach his resting place. Luckily for you, I've already made the mixture."* He will then hand you his [mixture](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion%27s_Mixture "Skyrim:Nurelion's Mixture") and add a marker to your map. He will then explain that the White Phial is a legendary bottle, forged in the days when Skyrim was just starting its turn to ice. He then tells you he spent his entire life searching for it, in libraries and small villages, researching its location, and will explain the name of his store: *"I even named my shop after it, hoping that it might attract anyone who had heard of it. And now it's within my grasp... but the Eight, it seems, have chosen me for their amusement.... for in my current condition, I'll never be able to lay my hands on it."*

### The Forsaken

[Forsaken Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Cave "Skyrim:Forsaken Cave")

The map marker leads to [Forsaken Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Cave "Skyrim:Forsaken Cave"), a cave west of Windhelm, straight south of [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand"). Enter the premises and head down the icy slope to the east. Kill the leveled [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"), [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"), or [snow bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") as you go along and open the door to the west, leading to a cave inhabited by [draugr enemies](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). A tempting chest will be visible in a tunnel as you go along, but beware of the [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") triggering a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") above the chest. After a while, the surroundings will change into catacombs and more draugr will be revived and attack. Fight your way through the many tunnels and keep an eye out for a copy of the [quest-related](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts#The_Mirror "Skyrim:Rare Gifts") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Mirror](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mirror "Skyrim:The Mirror")* near a locked door leading to a chest with minor loot. The large northwestern room has three [flame sprout traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") and a hidden chest just before the next tunnel. Beware of yet another pressure plate triggering a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") and pick up some useful potions and ingots from the shelves before entering [Forsaken Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Crypt "Skyrim:Forsaken Crypt").

You enter the crypt to the sight of a large room in two levels, with an overhanging bridge above. A draugr will be patrolling a path next to another still resting just around the corner. A ranged attack can dispose of it without disturbing the other. On the second floor another draugr will be found in its sarcophagus just to the right of the bridge.

Locate the narrow tunnel to the northeast and make your way upstairs. After dispatching a patrolling draugr, a pair of Ancient Nordic Boots and a hide helmet can be found on a table at the end of a passage. Around the next corner, four burial urns can be found cemented into the ground. Two more urns can be found on the ground to the right of the opening just before you reach the bridge which overlooks the room you passed through before entering the tunnel.

As you cross the bridge dispatch the leveled draugr which will emerge from its sarcophagus on the right end of the platform, then claim the contents of the chest and shelves on the other side. Turn right and cross another bridge into the next room, where you will encounter two draugr and a huge [ceiling spike](/wiki/Skyrim:Ceiling_Spikes "Skyrim:Ceiling Spikes") trap located in the center. An expert-locked door will be located on the western wall leading to an unlocked chest with some minor loot. The room features two burial urns on the northern wall, and a portcullis leading to a caved in tunnel.

Carefully make your way around the spike trap and pass through the iron door on the other side. Cross the gated bridge which overlooks the two lower levels you passed previously. A patrolling draugr can be sniped with a ranged weapon as it passes the corner at the end of the tunnel. Another sleeping draugr will be standing just round the corner to the right of the fire pit as you enter the room. The same situation will occur with the next corner. A final draugr wight will be sleeping in a standing position to the left hand side of the iron doorway, which opens into a [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") trap on the other side.

As you pass through the blades, the draugr boss [Curalmil](/wiki/Skyrim:Curalmil "Skyrim:Curalmil") will burst out of his sarcophagus and attack, along with several leveled draugr enemies. Dispose of them all and find the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") for a word related to the [Marked for Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Marked_for_Death "Skyrim:Marked for Death") shout and a boss-leveled chest. Find the tunnel leading west behind the sarcophagus and place [Nurelion's mixture](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion%27s_Mixture "Skyrim:Nurelion's Mixture") in the ancient bowl at the end. This lowers the stone wall in front of you and you will have free access to the final chamber which contains a variety of different alchemy ingredients, the alchemy skill book *[A Game at Dinner](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Game_at_Dinner "Skyrim:A Game at Dinner")*, and the [Cracked White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Cracked_White_Phial "Skyrim:Cracked White Phial"). Go back to the chamber with the word wall and turn right, where you will find an open set of iron doors leading to a staircase which will return you to [Forsaken Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Cave "Skyrim:Forsaken Cave"). As you enter the next room, activate the lever which will open the cavern wall and continue forward until you reach the tunnel leading back to Skyrim.

### The Crack in the Plan

Time is running out...

Back in The White Phial, Nurelion's poor health has taken yet another turn for the worse, forcing the old proprietor to sit in a chair around the clock with Quintus Navale in charge of the merchant services. Enter the private quarters upstairs and show Nurelion the cracked Phial. Understandably, this will make him quite upset: *"This... it matches every description of the Phial that I've found in lore. But if it can't hold liquid, there's no way of knowing. How did you manage to damage it, then? This is what I get for not retrieving it myself."* When you tell him that it was broken to begin with, he will become disparaging: *"Figures—I doubt you have sufficient knowledge to harm the Phial even if you wanted to. Either way, this is the end of it. Now if you'll excuse me, I'm not quite in the mood to entertain guests. I trust you can show yourself out. Here's for your trouble."* He then hands you a rather lousy reward of five gold, and then goes directly to bed, where he will stay 24 hours a day, obviously dying from his terminal illness. Attempting to speak to him after that will cause a "Nurelion is asleep and dying." message to appear on the screen, with an "OK" option directly below it.

Leave him and head downstairs where Quintus will be eager to talk to you: *"I want to thank you for your help. I know my master can be a bit short at times."* He will then make up for his master's cheapness and hand you an additional five hundred gold, then go to watch over his master upstairs. However, there's still hope. A few days later, you will receive a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Letter from Quintus Navale") from Quintus, starting the quest [Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial"). If, however, [The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World") is not yet completed before this quest, you'll first have to finish that one before you can start Repairing the Phial.

## Notes

- If you have a Numbers Job (Thieves Guild) for the White Phial active, complete it (return to Delvin Mallory) before completing the White Phial quest, or Nurelion's death will count as killing the target and failing the quest.

## Bugs

- The Phial can disappear if you leave the dungeon without taking it.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- At the completion of the quest, even when "asleep and dying" on his bed, you can still hear Nurelion continuing his standard dialogue about not liking loiterers and those who gawk at his goods.
- It is possible to receive double the amount that Quintus gives you as a reward from 500 to 1000 gold. Often when you finish the initial dialogue with Nurelion too quickly (without exiting during middle of the dialogue), he will repeat the same dialogue if you do not exit the second dialogue, which would result in a duplication of the 500 gold rewarded.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Quintus may not talk to Nurelion, making it impossible to start the next quest.
- If you don't enter the White Phial the first time that you enter Windhelm, it may be possible that Nurelion will be already dying in his bed when you visit him later. The quest cannot be started and his apprentice will not be available as merchant. **?**

## Quest Stages

| The White Phial (MS12) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | The alchemist of Windhelm, Nurelion, has asked me to find the legendary White Phial for him. *Objective 10:* Retrieve the White Phial |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Bring the Phial to Nurelion |
| 21 |  | *Objective 21:* Speak to Quintus |
| 100 | ☑ | I retrieved the White Phial for Nurelion, but it was damaged beyond repair. His assistant, Quintus, still paid me my reward, though. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS12 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS12`.

The Winking Skeever

**The Winking Skeever** is an [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") and bar found in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). It is the first building on the left-hand side when entering Solitude from the southwest. The name of the inn is proudly displayed on a sign adorning its front door. When asked about it, the owner, [Corpulus Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpulus_Vinius "Skyrim:Corpulus Vinius"), says that it was named for a childhood pet [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") that was said to be able to wink. If Corpulus dies, his son, [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius"), will take over renting out the inn's rooms, but Sorex will not buy or sell food (see [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius#Bugs "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius")).

[Gulum-Ei](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") [fences](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)") goods from his regular table if you have progressed far enough in the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") quest line.

Several citizens will point you toward the Winking Skeever. If you meet Sorex Vinius outside the tavern, he will say: *"New in town, right? If you need a place to sleep, head over to the Winking Skeever. We keep a fine inn."* and *"You know, the Winking Skeever's not just the best inn in Solitude. It's the also the only inn in Solitude."* [Vivienne Onis](/wiki/Skyrim:Vivienne_Onis "Skyrim:Vivienne Onis") will tell you: *"Most people head over to the Winking Skeever. If you're not interested in music or drink, you can at least talk to Corpulus. He can fill you in on any of the latest gossip."* Most [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard "Skyrim:Solitude Guard") in Solitude will also recommend the Winking Skeever: *"The Winking Skeever's got warm beds and cold mead. You look like you could use both."* [Lisette](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisette "Skyrim:Lisette"), the bard employed at the tavern, will also mention the place: *"Come by the Winking Skeever any time you want to hear a tune."* and *"You should think about staying the night. Corpulus keeps a clean inn."* and will add: *"Generally, if you want rumors, you should talk to Corpulus."* Outside Solitude, a few people will mention the Winking Skeever as well. In Dragon Bridge, Corpulus' cousin Faida will tell you: *"I was a barmaid at the Winking Skeever when I met my husband, rest his soul. Wasn't for him, I'd still be working there!"* [Thaer](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaer "Skyrim:Thaer"), the carriage driver outside Solitude, will also tell you: *"If you need it, you can get a room for a fair price at the Winking Skeever, just inside the main gate."* Most notably, [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") will send you to the Winking Skeever to meet [Malborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Malborn "Skyrim:Malborn") during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"): *"I'll get word for him to meet you in Solitude, at the Winking Skeever -- you know it?"*

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Belrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Belrand "Skyrim:Belrand") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Brina Merilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis") ‡  [Corpulus Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpulus_Vinius "Skyrim:Corpulus Vinius") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Galtius](/wiki/Skyrim:Galtius "Skyrim:Galtius") \*\*  [Gulum-Ei](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") [Fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Fence") \*  [Horik Halfhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Horik_Halfhand "Skyrim:Horik Halfhand") ‡  [Leyathil](/wiki/Skyrim:Leyathil "Skyrim:Leyathil") \*\*  [Lisette](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisette "Skyrim:Lisette") ([Bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Performances "Skyrim:Bardic Performances"))  [Marina](/wiki/Skyrim:Marina "Skyrim:Marina") \*\*  [Minette Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Minette_Vinius "Skyrim:Minette Vinius")  [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") † |

\* This person becomes a [fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)") after completing [Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly").
\*\* If they survive [Guests for Dinner](/wiki/Skyrim:Guests_for_Dinner "Skyrim:Guests for Dinner") on non-Vampire side.
† This person becomes innkeeper if Corpulus is dead.
‡ Will be exiled here if [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") is given to the [Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") in [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") and subsequently retaken by the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").

## Related Quests

- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery_(Sorex) "Skyrim:Delivery (Sorex)")**: Deliver a bottle of Rum to [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard").
- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").
- **[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless "Skyrim:The Restless")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread"): Search for an ancient pirate ship.
- **[Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly")**: Squeeze a [reluctant informer](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") for information.

## The Winking Skeever

Corpulus Vinius greets the Dragonborn to the Inn

The entrance leads directly into a large common room where part of it has a vaulted ceiling while the center is double height with a wooden balcony above. There are wooden benches, flower pots containing [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flowers and pillars supporting the vaulted ceiling around the edge of the center of the room. Directly in front of you is the counter in front of the northwest wall. There is an alcove in the southwest wall, where [Gulum-Ei](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") sits. The innkeeper, [Corpulus Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpulus_Vinius "Skyrim:Corpulus Vinius") stands behind the counter and greets customers. On the counter is a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and of [spiced wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:Spiced Wine"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and several pieces of cheese. To the right of the counter is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") driven into a block of wood. [Minette Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Minette_Vinius "Skyrim:Minette Vinius") will often be seen helping out, sweeping up, etc.

Behind the counter are two stacked open crates each containing five bottles of spiced wine, with a small set of shelves on either side holding several [empty bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"), a few sacks of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and three more bottles of spiced wine. Hanging from racks above these are five [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). In the western corner is another alcove storing a couple of food barrels, a few more food sacks and two sets of shelves hold a couple of [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") containing [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), three bottles of wine, five bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and several more empty bottles. To the right of the counter are three tables, one of which has a couple of loose septims on it, around a cooking fire with a stone chimney with two openings at eye level, on the near side is a piece of [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef") and a cast iron pot containing a cabbage and a potato, while around on the other side is an empty metal pot.

Gulum-Ei enjoys his little corner of the inn

In the alcove where Gulum-Ei sits is a small table and chair, with a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and a couple of loaves of bread on the table. There is a narrow table against the rear wall with a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") in a soul gem holder on top, while against the northwest wall of the alcove is a small cupboard with shelves above holding a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing").

A view of the balcony

In the center of the room are four more small tables, two of which are laid with two plates holding salmon steaks, one is laid a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat") and the final table is where [Belrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Belrand "Skyrim:Belrand") normally sits available for hire as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") for 500 [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). His table has a bottle of wine and a plate of bread and cheese on it. There is also a long wooden table in the eastern corner of the room with another sweet roll and two more honey nut treats. There are two wall shelves along the northeast wall, one holds a couple of empty wine bottles while the other has a giant's club, that can't be taken. Nearly opposite this is a small cupboard with a [platter](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter") holding two baked potatoes, a sweet roll and a couple of pieces of cheese.

There is a wide corridor to the northeast with a narrow table along the northwest wall, with another salmon steak on top and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") beside it. Opposite this on the southeast wall is a door into a bedroom used by [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius"), it contains a single bed in the eastern corner with a side table at the foot of it holding a bottle of alto wine. Next to this along the northeast wall is a narrow wooden table holding a bowl containing a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") and a bulb of garlic. To the left as you enter, against the northwest wall is a small wardrobe with shelves above it holding a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), a potion of healing and a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"). Beside this is a basket containing a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") and a few sacks of food. Against the southeast wall is an end table with a copy of *[Shezarr and the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shezarr_and_the_Divines "Skyrim:Shezarr and the Divines")*, while against the southwest wall is a tall wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and a wall shelf holding a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), a loaf of bread and some cheese. Under this is a long table and chair. On this table are a couple of bottles of wine, a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), bunch of lavender and a platter holding two baked potatoes, a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), a sweet roll and a couple of pieces of cheese.

At the end of the corridor, where it turns to the northwest is a set of shelves in the eastern corner holding a potion of minor healing and two potions of healing. The corridor leads to a stairwell with stairs up to the top floor and down to the cellar. At the top of the stairs in a large landing with a balcony looking down into the center of the room below. On the left at the top of the stairs is another set of shelves holding a potion of minor healing and two potions of healing. At the other end of the northeast wall is a narrow table with a [chaurus egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), a [hagraven claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw") and a stone bowl containing a bunch of lavender, a bulb of garlic, a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), a [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"). Along the southeast wall are two doors leading to bedrooms with a low table between them. To the southwest is the balcony with two tables and chairs, the first table is set with a bottle of wine, a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") and a plate of bread. The second is holding a plate of bread and cheese with a bottle of wine, a goblet and a copy of *[The Cake and The Diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cake_and_The_Diamond "Skyrim:The Cake and The Diamond")*. There are also two bookcases next to this against the northwest wall holding seven more common books, a master-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength") and a [potion of extreme stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Stamina"). To the right of these is a small wardrobe with the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") on top.

The room available for rent

The bedroom to the left is L-shaped and contains a single bed at the southeastern end of the room with a low table and chair beside it, there's a copy of *[The Real Barenziah, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Real_Barenziah,_v3 "Skyrim:The Real Barenziah, v3")* on the table and above the table, on the southwest wall are two wall shelves holding a bunch of lavender and a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing"). To the right, along the same wall is a tall wardrobe. At the northeastern end of the room is another tall wardrobe, a narrow table against the southeast wall with a bottle of wine and two honey nut treats on it and opposite are two bookcases holding eleven common books, a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), a solution of strength and a potion of extreme stamina. The bedroom on the right is the room you get shown to if you rent a room, which contains a large double bed coming out from the southeast wall with an end table to the left holding a bottle of wine and a common book. There is a long unlocked chest at the foot of the bed. Against the northeast wall are two small wardrobes with a washbasin on a stand between them. On them are a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug"), a goblet, and a platter holding a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), a couple of loaves of bread and a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"). To the right of the bed, against the southwest wall is a long wooden table with a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a potion of health, a potion of regeneration, a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength") and a drum. To the right of this, coming out from the same wall are two bookcases holding a [potion of extreme magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Magicka"), nine common books and copies of two less common books; *[Charwich-Koniinge Letters, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge_Letters,_v1 "Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge Letters, v1")* and *[Amongst the Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Amongst_the_Draugr "Skyrim:Amongst the Draugr")*. On the other side of the bookcases is a wooden bench and a low table holding a platter with a bunch of lavender on it and a common book. In the western corner is a tall wardrobe with a narrow wooden table to the right with another common book and a bowl of [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") on it.

Descending the stairs to the cellar, at the bottom of the stairs is a dresser against the southwest wall with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top. The rest of the cellar is heavily vaulted with an alcove just after the dresser on the same wall containing two sets of shelves holding twenty-eight more empty wine bottles--(see [notes](#Notes)). Straight ahead in the cellar is a large vat with two more alcoves, one to the northeast and the other to the southwest. The first of these has a couple of large vats at either end with some food barrels behind the one to the left. In front is a wooden table and a couple of chairs. The other alcove, to the southwest has a cupboard holding a bottle of each alto wine and wine, while the alcove continues to the left. At the southeast end is a cupboard holding clutter and two sets of shelves, one holding an iron dagger and a couple of pieces of cheese and the other holding a bottle of wine and two bottles of Nord mead, it also has an unlocked chest on top.

Outside, along the northeast wall is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and at the back along the same wall is one of three [thieves caches](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_Cache "Skyrim:Thief Cache") found in each major city once you have completed the relevant [reputation quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Reputation_quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"). It is a barrel marked with  "Cache") Cache [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)").

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the Winking Skeever's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 7 | Random [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |
| 10 | Random inn food |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |

## Notes

- There are three [shadowmarks](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") found here:
  - A  "Fence") Fence shadowmark is next to [Gulum-Ei](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") as he is a [Fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)").
  - A  "Loot") Loot shadowmark is to the bottom left of the entrance door.
  - A  "Cache") Cache shadowmark is on a barrel on the northeast wall of the building after completing the relevant quest.
- Completing the [Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery_(Sorex) "Skyrim:Delivery (Sorex)") quest for [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius") makes low value items freely available, including two beds that will grant the [Well Rested](/wiki/Skyrim:Well_Rested "Skyrim:Well Rested") bonus, (but not the rentable bed).
- There are a total of at least 56 empty wine bottles available for free as long as you have completed the above quest. These can be used at the [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") to make [Conjurer's Elixir](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer%27s_Elixir "Skyrim:Conjurer's Elixir").
- Version 1.3.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") allows 3 crew members from the [Red Wave](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave") to come to the inn, making them available for brawl targets, and enabling several lines of unique dialogue that otherwise would have been unavailable.
- The Winking Skeever appears as [The Lonely Troll](/wiki/Online:The_Lonely_Troll "Online:The Lonely Troll") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The [Potion of Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing") you find on the ground outside is not where it's supposed to be. You're supposed to find it on one of the exterior windows on the upper floor, but a bug prevented that from being the case. **?**
